U.S. Commercial and Industrial Conditions 58

A Thriving Sign

[Washington] The Federal Reserve Board today issued a summary of the national business conditions, proving that U.S. industry is now showing a thriving sign. Production is now trending upwards, with rapid development in December last year. This continued to grow throughout January and the first half of February this year. The index at 31st January reached 90 percent of the average for 1932, 1924 and 1925. This is the highest point since 1933. Production in December last year was 86 percent, an increase of 8 percent compared to January of last year. This was due to increased automobile production, and increased winter employment in factories was also a factor. However, general construction remains lagging behind. The authorities are excited about this improvement, but are also unwilling to comment on future trends. Since the gold clause ruling, business activity has not increased as expected, which is disappointing to many. Some say that the uncertain outlook for legislation is the reason. Commercial recovery depends on heavy industry, but heavy industry remains sluggish. The work relief program, which is considered to revitalize basic industries, is now facing an uncertain fate. According to Wall Street experts, market rallies are unlikely to occur until the work relief bill and other political issues are resolved. However, the general commercial situation is still fairly satisfactory. (Reuters dispatch dated the 26th)

Cause of U.S. Airship Disaster 59

Navy Doesn't Trust Experts' Theories

[Washington] Senior naval officials here today expressed little confidence in the theory put forward by airship expert Dr. Klemin that the crash of the airship Macon was caused by sabotage of the machinery. Rear Admiral King, Chief of the Bureau of Aeronautics, told the licensing committee investigating the airship crash that he did not believe the incident involved sabotage of the machinery. Although sabotage of the machinery is always possible, I really do not believe that this time was related to sabotage. Captain Wiley, the captain of the Macon, previously stated that Dr. Klemin's claim of pouring corrosive acids on metal plates was impossible because the Macon was heavily guarded and inspections were carried out frequently. Dr. Klemin still believes that the cause of the Macon's crash was sabotage of the machinery. Dr. Klemin said today that Captain Wiley should know that it only takes a minute to pour enough acid on the metal plates to completely disable the airship, and then in another minute, the perpetrator can escape unnoticed on board. It is said that the House Licensing Committee will continue to investigate the cause of the incident, and its conclusions will have a significant impact on Congress's decision on whether the United States should build more large military airships in the future. Secretary of the Navy Swanson has stated that he personally does not want to support the continued construction of large airships, but some officials are asking the government to subsidize the construction of one or more national airships. It is reported that the Congressional committee will also study the possibility of this matter. (Guomin News Agency dispatch dated the 26th)

General Assembly of the League of Nations Meets in September: China is Expected to Be Elected to a Council Seat 60

[Geneva] The League of Nations General Assembly will discuss the issue of re-electing China as a council member of the League of Nations in September. It is widely believed that China has a good chance of being elected. Since Japan's withdrawal from the League, there has been no country representing Asia on the Administrative Council. Turkey often considers itself a European country, so it cannot be truly regarded as an Asian country. Although there is no question of China succeeding Japan and occupying a permanent council seat, there is a feeling that a new permanent or non-permanent council seat should be added so that the number of members of the Administrative Council is not lacking, and this new seat should naturally belong to China. South America, including Mexico, occupies three seats on the Administrative Council. The League of Nations feels that the distribution is uneven and is studying ways to remedy this. Guo Taiqi, the Chinese Ambassador to the United Kingdom, said in an interview with a Reuters reporter today that when China failed to be re-elected last September, he explained these reasons to the representatives of various countries in the League of Nations. He now understands that the executive department of the British League of Nations Union is now strongly urging Geneva to re-elect China as a council member of the Administrative Council. (Reuters dispatch dated the 27th)

If Europe Is in Trouble, Italy Is Ready and Prepared 61

Eight Million Soldiers Can Be Mobilized Immediately

Publishing a Communiqué is No Less Than a Warning to Germany

Will Resolutely Exercise National Power Over the Weak and Small in East Africa

[Rome] The government recently issued a communiqué stating that, in addition to the reservists of the 1911 class who have been mobilized and sent to East Africa, it does not intend to further conscript reservists into the army. This communiqué is sufficient to ease people's minds. Recently, there have been rumors everywhere that the government will launch a large-scale conscription of reservists to be sent to the north to prevent incidents on the Austrian border. The Supreme Defence Council recently issued a communiqué stating that if a war were to break out, Italy would be ready and prepared, and people's minds began to calm down slightly. The government's communiqué issued today also stated that the Franco-Italian agreement of January 7 and the Anglo-French agreement of February 3, in which Italy indirectly participated, created a foundation for a security system. Italy's participation in this security system also applies to other regions of Europe. Although the claim that Italian troops are concentrated near the Brenner Pass has been repeatedly denied by the authorities, the authorities have always demanded that Italy has the right to set up garrisons in the border area. Although the communiqué issued today did not mention the risk of disputes arising in the current European situation, it is indeed a serious warning to those who seek to disrupt the current international order, indicating that if necessary, the Pan-Italic government will intervene without hesitation. (Havas dispatch dated the 26th)

[Paris] The Italian government issued a communiqué yesterday to explain the dispatch of troops to the East African territory of Eritrea, stating that Italy is ready and prepared in both Africa and Europe. The Reuters dispatch from yesterday has already covered this. The Rome correspondent of "Le Petit Parisien" added a commentary, saying that "the Italian government recognizes the Rome and London agreements" as the foundation for the peaceful development of international relations. However, should unexpected changes occur in the European situation, Italy is also prepared for Germany. A reporter from "Le Matin" also made the same argument, saying that "Although Italy is preparing to develop its colonies, its potential military strength is not weakened as a result. If Europe is in trouble, Italy is prepared to deal with everything. Italy's friendly assurance to Britain and France is, at the same time, a solemn declaration to Germany, and its intention is nothing more than this." According to the communiqué issued by the Italian government, Italy can mobilize seven to eight million regular troops in times of crisis. (Havas dispatch dated the 26th)

[Rome] "Italy can mobilize eight million soldiers in a very short period of time." This was the warning in the communiqué issued by the Italian government when it dispatched troops from various ports to Italian Somaliland. Officials do not regard this statement as a show of intimidation, but as a formal warning to the small state of Abyssinia, urging it to be prudent and to know that the European powers will never allow themselves to be played with, as the Abyssinian officials are currently adopting an indifferent attitude. The communiqué stated, "It should be known that the current Pan-Italic law forces all men aged 18 to 55 to serve in the military, so Italy can mobilize 37 classes of troops, totaling seven to eight million people." To prevent incidents on the Somaliland border, two divisions have been re-mobilized and concentrated in Naples, ready to depart at any time. "However, Italy's dispatch of troops to Africa is only to increase the defense of the two territories of Somaliland and Eritrea." According to official announcements, Italy has sent tens of thousands of troops to East Africa in the past two weeks. Some observers believe that today's communiqué is intended to warn the Abyssinian King that his 100,000 soldiers cannot resist Italy's millions of well-equipped troops. (Guomin News Agency dispatch dated the 26th)

Three Battalions of the Italian Fascist Party Arrive in East Africa. [Rome] One battalion of the three battalions of the Pan-Italic Fascist Party army heading to East Africa has arrived in East Africa. However, the "Vinci," which transported troops from the port of Messina to East Africa, has delayed its departure due to bad weather. (Havas dispatch dated the 26th)

[Rome] The Abyssinian Chargé d'Affaires declared during a visit to Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs Suvich that Abyssinia was prepared to abandon its demand that the Swedish and Belgian investigation teams currently in the country participate in negotiations to demarcate a six-kilometer neutral zone between Abyssinia and Italian Somaliland. This investigation team is purely military in nature. The Italian government has already approved this new proposal and has agreed to allow nomadic peoples to enter and exit the area and use the water from the wells there. Italy has not yet commented on Abyssinia's suggestion to invoke the arbitration clause in the Italo-Abyssinian Peace Treaty. Italy is still actively transporting troops and armaments to Italian Somaliland. Italian newspapers believe that this is a necessary step to ensure safety. (Guomin News Agency dispatch dated the 26th)

Arabs Serve Italy. Milan, Italy: According to reports from here, Italy has a very large indigenous volunteer army in Eritrea, East Africa, which is the largest in the cities around the Red Sea. These people are mostly Arab Muslim warriors, as well as farmers, herdsmen, and miners from British Somaliland. (Guomin News Agency dispatch dated the 26th)

[Rome] Italian Colonial Commander Graziani expressed his views on European operations in Africa. Graziani is a major authority on Italian colonial affairs. Regarding European and indigenous armies, he advocated using more indigenous troops. Firstly, indigenous people are accustomed to the hardships of the tropical climate, while European troops require supplies and replenishment, which are indispensable in every aspect. To achieve perfection, there must be a perfect organization, but this is especially difficult to achieve in guerrilla warfare in Africa. As for the transportation costs of the troops, they are even more enormous. Just looking at the transportation costs in the Suez Canal, it costs 25 francs per person to pass through this canal, and other transportation costs are even greater. Therefore, the use of troops in the colonies is not as good as using indigenous people. (Guomin News Agency dispatch dated the 26th)

Sweden Avoids Getting Involved in the Vortex. The Swedish officers serving as military instructors in Abyssinia have been ordered by the Swedish government not to undertake other missions in Abyssinia, unless they receive special instructions from the Swedish government. It is reported that Abyssinia requested that one Swedish and one Belgian officer participate in the demarcation committee for the neutral zone, but this was rejected by Italy. The Swedish government's order is a response to this rumor. (Havas dispatch dated the 26th)

Seeking Help from Major Powers Achieved: Austrian Prime Minister Quietly Leaves England and Returns Home 62

Gained Sympathy for Solving Financial Difficulties

Indicated that Austrian Restoration is Currently Necessary

[London] Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Berger were escorted by police tonight under tight security and departed in a highly confidential manner to return to Austria. Schuschnigg and Berger carried back to Vienna the responses of the British and French diplomatic authorities regarding the future of Austria. For a week, the two met repeatedly with British and French authorities. They announced that they had reached an agreement with France. As for their secret departure from England, it was to prevent communist demonstrations, so there was a large police presence at the station to protect them. The car they were travelling in was specially hidden. Those who went to the station to see them off included the Austrian Ambassador to the United Kingdom, Fürstenberg, British Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs Vansittart, and representatives of Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon. (Guomin News Agency dispatch dated the 26th)

[London] Before Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Berger left England, Schuschnigg hosted British and other foreign journalists at the Austrian Embassy, ​​but did not mention the real mission of their trip to England. He only said that they had gained the other party's sympathy to solve many difficult problems, such as the loans handled by the League of Nations. He then described the political and economic situation of Austria and vigorously demonstrated how prosperous the financial prospects of Austria after its independence would be. When the Austrian guests left London, there were strict precautions taken to prevent accidents. Schuschnigg also met with the Italian Ambassador to the United Kingdom while in London. (Guomin News Agency dispatch dated the 27th)

Centered on the Danube River Convention, Seeking Political and Economic Stability in Central Europe 63

[London] Before returning to his country, Austrian Foreign Minister Berger told a reporter from "Le Matin" in Paris: "We are not here to beg for alms. What we are discussing is the political stability and economic recovery of Central Europe based on the Danube River Convention. We oppose not only the political Anschluss with Germany, but also the economic Anschluss with Germany. After coming here, we have enabled the British government to have a clearer understanding of the situation in Austria, which we are very pleased with." (Havas dispatch dated the 27th)

The Austrian Government Extremely Opposed the Inclusion of a Clause Prohibiting Restoration 64

[London] Before Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Berger departed to return home, they had a long conversation with Italian Ambassador to the United Kingdom Grandi. Afterwards, the Austrian cabinet members crossed the English Channel in Boulogne and then transferred to a special express train, via Basel, Switzerland, to return to Vienna. The government took various important measures to avoid accidents at the time of departure. After the Austrian cabinet members departed, well-informed sources announced that if the Danube River Convention included a clause prohibiting the restoration of the Habsburg dynasty, it would be extremely opposed by the Austrian government. In addition, Prime Minister Schuschnigg said in response to press inquiries that the Austrian restoration is currently necessary because it is impossible to restore economic prosperity without restoration. (Havas dispatch dated the 26th)

Austrian Prime Minister Issues Declaration After Returning Home

[Vienna] Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg declared to a reporter from the "Neue Freie Presse" that the word "Monarch" was not mentioned in the talks in Paris and London. The adoption of any political system in Austria is purely an internal affair. The Austrian authorities have a deep understanding of their responsibilities and are determined not to cause incidents that would harm the peace of Central Europe, or even the whole of Europe. This can be seen from this declaration. (Havas dispatch dated the 27th)

Budapest, Hungary. Panama Refuses to Accept US Check for Canal Zone Rent 70

Cash to be Paid According to Lease

Panama: The US government recently paid the Panamanian government a check for $250,000 as the annual fee for the use of the Panama Canal Zone. Today, the Panamanian government returned the original check with a note stating that according to the land lease treaty, the rent must be paid in cash and cannot be paid in "devalued currency." If the US government does not pay in cash, the Panamanian government will default on the $16 million in Panamanian bonds held by the United States. In November of last year, the Panamanian government had already refused to accept the check, but the Panamanian government has been paying the bonds held by the United States on time. The Panama Canal area was leased to the United States in 1904 by contract, with an initial compensation fee of $10 million and a fixed annual rent of $250,000. (Reuters dispatch, 26th)

Considering What to Do About Paraguay's Withdrawal from the League

Some poison gas has been transported to the front. Therefore, the Bolivian General Staff has ordered the Air Force to immediately retaliate if the enemy uses poison gas. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

[Geneva] The Advisory Committee established by the League of Nations Assembly for the Chaco dispute is scheduled to meet on March 11 to prepare for a study of how to deal with Paraguay's withdrawal from the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch, 27th)

Northeast Soybean Production Declines Under Japanese Military Rule 110

US Soybean Cultivation Successful, Inevitable Competition with Manchurian Beans

Changchun Dispatch: Northeast soybean production has always occupied a leading position in international trade. Since the September 18th Incident, the Northeast has been in a state of mixed warfare between the Volunteer Army and the Japanese puppet army. In addition, in the past two years, floods have affected various regions, and the rural economy has reached the point of bankruptcy. Soybean production has also declined as a result. Recently, the results of soybean cultivation in various European and American countries have also tended to improve. Countries such as the United States, Hungary, Czechoslovakia, and Germany all account for a considerable proportion of annual production. Among them, the United States has the highest production. In 1932, it exported 112,700 tons, accounting for one-fifth of the Northeast soybean exports in the same year. Last year, soybeans imported into Japan from "Manchuria" accounted for one-fifth of the total "Manchurian" production, and soybean oil exports to Japan accounted for about three-quarters. The Northeast soybean imports to Europe and the world soybean production, as well as the import volume of various countries, are listed as follows:

As shown in the table above, the United States has achieved the best results in soybean cultivation. Previously, the production was only enough to meet domestic needs. Recently, production has increased and imports to Europe have also accounted for a considerable proportion. Judging from the recent situation, the United States is making more efforts in soybean cultivation and seed improvement, and claims that it can compete with "Manchuria" to compensate for the loss of US wheat production. In the event that US soybeans surpass "Manchuria," the "Manchurian" soybeans under Japanese puppet management will suffer a great blow. (Northeast News Agency)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Receives Senior Civil and Military Officials 111

Telegraphs Sichuan Provincial Government to Take Over Various Generals' Garrison Areas, Expeditionary Headquarters Established as Scheduled, Personnel Designated for Various Positions

Hankou Dispatch: Chairman Chiang Kai-shek crossed the Yangtze River at 9:00 AM on the 25th to attend the expanded memorial week of the Three-Province Bandit Suppression Headquarters, and gave a very earnest speech (full text being organized). He then received Zhang Xueliang, Qian Dajun, He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Huang Musong, Chen Cheng, Yu Xuezhong, Wan Fulin, Wang Shuchang, Miao Chengliu, Guo Xipeng, Huang Xiansheng, etc., and inquired about military and political affairs. Huang Musong reported the details of his trip to Tibet. After leaving the headquarters, Chiang inspected the Provincial Government and then returned to Hankou. The Wuchang Expeditionary Headquarters will be formally established on the first day of next month. In addition to Zhang Xueliang as Director of the Expeditionary Headquarters, Qian Dajun as Chief of Staff, and Yang Yongtai as Secretary-General, which were decided earlier, the candidates for the seven directly subordinate departments have also been designated. Generally speaking, the Director of the First Department is Yan Xunfu, the Director of the Second Department is Xiong Zhongtao, the Director of the Third Department is Mi Chunlin, the Director of the Fourth Department is Wu Jiaxiang, the Director of the Fifth Department is Gan Naiguang, the Director of the Sixth Department is Wen Qun, or Chen Longxian, and the Director of the Seventh Department is concurrently held by Yang Yongtai. The above departments are directed by the Chief of Staff and Secretary-General. In addition, there are four departments under the control of the Expeditionary Headquarters, such as He Zhonghan, Director of the Political Training Department, and Lin Xiang, Director of the Transportation Department, who are both incumbents. In addition, the Chairman's Adjutant's Office has one or two departments. The Director of the First Department is Yan Daogang, and the Director of the Second Department is Chen Bulei. It is rumored that there is also a Military Affairs Reorganization Department (the name seems to be undetermined). The position of Director will be assigned to Chen Cheng. They are not subordinate to the Expeditionary Headquarters. Whether there will be any further changes is unknown.

Chairman Chiang expressed his appreciation to the Sichuan military generals for breaking up their defense zones and returning political power. He has telegraphed the Sichuan Provincial Government and various military generals to discuss the methods of taking over the garrison areas, transfer them as soon as possible, and report back. The original telegram is as follows: (Sichuan has been in turmoil for many years, and the military and the people are suffering. The special system of defense zones is not a good thing. The political function has lost its power to operate, and the social economy has fallen into collapse, causing the people to be blamed for feudalism and giving the enemy an excuse for disorganization. As a result, the Red bandits took the opportunity to use it as a haven for escape. Xu and Zhang have been entrenched on the north bank, and Zhu and Mao have repeatedly disturbed the southern border. Although it is fortunate that the various armies have fought bravely and encircled them, and there is hope of driving away the ugly, bandit suppression must use seven points of politics, which has become an unbreakable trend. Then the army is trying its best to suppress the bandits in a local area, while politics is universally creating bandits invisibly. The so-called fox buries and fox digs, its ridiculous contradiction, how can it be more than this. Now that the provincial government has been reorganized and established, and the generals of the various armies have successively declared to break up the defense zones and return political power, it can be seen that things must be reversed, and new opportunities have arisen, which is commendable. However, moving to good is valuable in doing, and eliminating abuses should be quick. It is hoped that the provincial government and the generals of the various armies will discuss the methods of taking over the garrison areas, transfer them as soon as possible, and report back without any hesitation. From now on, the provincial government is responsible for improving politics, and the generals are dedicated to reorganizing the army, gathering the achievements of unification, and gradually creating a healthy and prosperous governance. The revival of Sichuan is the foundation for the revival of the Chinese nation. The provincial government and the generals have heavy responsibilities, and they should all work hard. Seal of Chiang Kai-shek) (25th)

Jiangxi Province Gradually Lifts Blockade 112

—Salt Monopoly Taken Over by Cooperatives—

Nanchang Dispatch: The Red bandits in the hinterland of Jiangxi can be said to be completely suppressed. In the border areas bordering neighboring provinces and the remote mountainous areas between counties, there are inevitably still scattered bandits hiding and resisting, waiting to be suppressed and pacified at the same time in order to eradicate them. However, at the beginning of the fifth encirclement and suppression, the policy of encirclement, blockade, blockhouses, and transportation was used to kill the bandits. Now that the bandits have been suppressed, the blockade should be lifted to allow goods to flow smoothly. The Expeditionary Headquarters has previously formulated a method of gradually advancing towards the bandit areas from the safe areas and lifting the blockade. That is, the blockade can be lifted in areas where the village cleaning and baojia have been completed and there are no traces of bandits within four borders, and the trade of grain, salt, kerosene, and cloth can be freely traded and restored to its original state. In the newly recovered areas where the remaining bandits have not yet been eliminated, the blockade will still be tightened, and the Ministry of Civil Affairs will set up a blockade section to manage the matter. The Security Department will manage and control the transportation permits for the daily necessities of the good people in the recovered areas. According to news from Fuzhou and Nanfeng, the blockade in that area has been gradually lifted. However, salt is the most important of the daily necessities of the common people. The authorities are sincerely afraid that the salt merchants will manipulate the market and hoard goods, and the common people will be exploited. Therefore, the salt monopoly is uniformly handed over to the already established cooperatives for transportation and sales to reduce the burden on the people in the bandit areas. However, the Nanchang Salt Guild, concerned with its business life, held a meeting and decided to send a letter to all counties and cities to strive for it unanimously. (February 23rd)

Songjiang 113

Anti-Smoking Committee Searches for Unauthorized Smokers

Wang Jiajun, leader of the investigation team of the Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee in the Songjiang area, recently learned that the atmosphere of smoking is very strong in Zhalin, Xintang and other places in this county. On the 24th, he specially joined ten police officers from Fengxian County and first went to the Cao Yiji smoking shop in Zhalin to inspect. It was found that the shop had a Class C license, but had ten opium pipes, and there were nine smokers inside, which was a violation of the regulations. He immediately asked the smokers to show their smoking cessation licenses. They all hesitated. Later, the owner took out a Class A smoking cessation license and twelve Class B smoking cessation licenses from the counter. As a result, after verification by Commissioner Wang, two of them matched the photos and were released immediately. The remaining seven have been sent to Songjiang yesterday, and the four smokers and twenty-one pieces of smoking paraphernalia seized from Xia Jianzhong's house in Xintang Town have also been sent to Songjiang for the Anti-Smoking Committee to handle. In addition, the investigators of the County Anti-Smoking Committee, Sun Zongxiang, and the police of the Second Substation searched the Qinji smoking shop in this city yesterday and found three unlicensed smokers, including Chen Xiannian, the home brewing tax collection director of the county's tobacco and alcohol tax office. He has also been transferred to the Anti-Smoking Committee for verification.

Suzhou 114

Field Tax Corruption Case Sent to Court for Handling

Zhu Jingbo, the former director of the Wuxian County Field Tax Collection Office, was accused of seven counts, including privately promoting tax collection, dereliction of duty and corruption, and embezzlement of people's arrears. The Finance Department dispatched Dong Binqian to Suzhou to investigate. Because it was found that Zhu did have corrupt behavior, Zhu was detained, dismissed, and was awaiting investigation. Later, at the end of the lunar year, Zhu was released on bail. Now the case has been investigated and completed. The Dong Committee, together with the Wuxian County magistrate, submitted the investigation process to the Finance Department in detail. According to provincial sources, Director Zhao believes that Zhu is suspected of corruption and will be transferred to the Wuxian County Local Court for investigation and handling in accordance with the law.

Wuxi 115

Provincial Committee Arrives in Wuxi to Investigate the Anti-Smoking Policy

The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee, in order to understand the implementation of the anti-smoking policy in various counties, specially dispatched instructor and investigator Mr. Qin Manyuan to investigate in various counties. After being commissioned, Mr. Qin first went to Wujin for inspection, and then went to Jiangyin for investigation. Now he came to Wuxi from Cheng. Yesterday, he went to the county government to meet with County Magistrate Yan, and went to the County Anti-Smoking Association to inquire about the implementation of the anti-smoking policy and the current work outline. Finally, Secretary Yao led him to inspect the drug rehabilitation center and the investigation team, which was very thorough. The reporter visited Investigator Qin at his residence and asked about ways to promote smokers' self-surrender. He talked about two points: (1) Use the Baojia system to obtain joint guarantees from each household in each Baojia, guaranteeing that there are no smokers in each household in each Baojia; (2) Use school students to individually promote to each parent, and first persuade the parents of students who use drugs to quit. If it is not effective, then give various ridicules and humiliations. In this way, students with smoking parents will inevitably have to earnestly persuade their parents in this environment, and the parents will have to automatically quit after being moved by this. It seems that it is easier to achieve results by doing this, and it is not difficult to eliminate the scourge of opium.

Failure to Affix Stamp Duty Sent to Court for Handling

The Ministry of Finance is very strict in the implementation of stamp duty. Regarding violations of regulations and tax evasion, it is stipulated that they should be sent to the court for handling. After receiving the order, the local county chamber of commerce has repeatedly notified all industries to affix stamps in accordance with the regulations to avoid suffering losses. Recently, Ju Da Nanhuo store in Badou Alley outside the North Gate sold a batch of goods to Xizhi Street, Changzhou. Its invoice was not affixed with the correct stamp duty, which was discovered by Changzhou and sent to the local branch court for handling. After receiving the letter, the court scheduled to summon the manager of the store, Gai Yaozu, to the court at 9:00 am today (the 28th) to investigate and handle the case.

Changzhou 116

Suzhou Militia Member Commits Suicide by Poison in Changzhou

A traveler came to the Huashang Hotel in Juqian Street, Wuyi on the 24th. He was wearing a gray uniform and had no luggage. He opened room No. 8 and filled in the traveler's form with the name Chen Yihong, from Jiangyin, 28 years old. The room rate for that room was 40 cents per day. At that time, he prepaid one silver dollar. He went out on the afternoon of the 25th and did not return to the inn until after 12 o'clock at night. At that time, the tea house thought he had returned from watching a play and did not suspect anything else. Unexpectedly, at about 6 o'clock on the morning of the 26th, he suddenly heard a groan in the room. He called him, but he did not respond. He was shocked and immediately opened the door and reported to the first branch of the Public Security Bureau. He was immediately sent to Wujin Hospital for treatment. After the doctor's diagnosis, it was found that he had taken raw opium. Although he tried his best to rescue him, he died of poisoning too deeply and died at about 3 o'clock in the afternoon. It was then discovered that the symbol worn by the traveler was a member of the first row of the first A of the second district of the Wuxian County Security Regiment. As for the reason for his suicide, he could not speak after taking the poison, and there was no suicide note, so there was no way to find out.

Changshu 117

Official Salt Boat Robbed, Five Bandits Arrested

Zhang Yuantai Salt Guild Hall outside Xiaodongmen in this county dispatched six boats the day before yesterday to Liouhe to load salt to Changshu. Among them, one boat suddenly stopped overnight near Dongtang City in this county because the sailors were weak. Unexpectedly, at 9 o'clock that night, nine bandits, armed with box cannons and other weapons, forced them to set sail. They started robbing near Qixing Bridge, and about two hundred bags were robbed, worth more than a thousand yuan. The next morning, the boat owner Yang Yongsheng went to the city to report to the public station, which was forwarded to the Public Security Bureau. The investigation team went to the scene of the incident to investigate. They then arrested Zhang Fuda, Zhou Er, Zhang Genxing, and Lu Er, who were selling stolen salt on behalf of others, in Sujia Weng, outside Xiaodongmen. On the 26th, they were sent to the county government. After interrogation, they were detained separately.

Nantong 118

Trafficking in Peasant Girls, Convicts Sentenced

The drought in the counties north of the Yangtze River is extremely severe. There are even human traffickers taking advantage of the opportunity to carry out large-scale activities, luring peasant girls and transporting them to the south of the Yangtze River for sale. Police detectives successively arrested the ringleaders in Tongjing and Wuxi, one was Xia Jiu, and the other was a young widow, Miss Chen Jin. They were escorted to the court together. The criminal court concluded the trial and pronounced the verdict on the 26th. Xia Jiu and Miss Chen Jin were each sentenced to five years in prison.

Since prison guard Chen Gang took office in the county prison, he has failed to strictly rectify the prisoners in custody. Recently, new prisoners have been extorted by old prisoners, and gambling is rampant in the prison. Old prisoners have been drawing profits from it. After someone reported to County Magistrate Yan, County Magistrate Yan and Trial Officer Jiang went to the prison for inspection on the afternoon of the 25th and instructed prison guard Chen to strictly rectify all prison affairs in the future, and to pay attention to hygiene because the prison was filthy and smelly.

Funing 121

Li Xueying Tragically Kills His Own Son

In Dakunli, Naxiang, this county, there is Li Xueying, who does not engage in proper business. He often quarrels with his father, Li Zhian, and steals his father's money. If he is not satisfied, he will threaten his father and will kill him in the future. Unexpectedly, Zhian thought that his son could speak and do things, so it is better to kill Xueying first to avoid future troubles. On the evening of the 16th of this month, he bought wine and got his son drunk, and killed him with a knife. The body was chopped into several pieces. He wrapped the body in reed mats and buried it in a mass grave on the seawall. Unexpectedly, yesterday, Liu, Xueying's uncle, and Zhao Jinrong, his cousin, looked for Xueying to collect debts. Liu went to Xueying's house and suddenly went crazy, shouting and running around, running to the mass grave, and opened the mud with his hands, and Xueying's body was exposed. His cousin, Zhao Jinrong, followed Liu here and saw several knife wounds on the body. Knowing that he was killed by his father, he questioned An and went to the county to report the case.

Local News

After the Auction of the Shenxin No. 7 Factory, the Authorities Negotiated with HSBC 122

The Huayin Consortium Decided to Appeal According to the Law

All Sectors of Industry and Commerce Unanimously Provided Assistance

According to the Central News Agency, the auction of the Shenxin Textile Company's No. 7 Factory by the British HSBC Bank to a Japanese company for 2.25 million yuan the day before yesterday not only stirred up a huge shock among our government authorities, financial and industrial circles, but also received unanimous support from the media. Therefore, the general public has been closely watching the development of this event. Yesterday, a Central News Agency reporter made a special trip to inquire about everything from all parties involved. The details are as follows:

Municipal Authorities Negotiated with HSBC. At 3:30 p.m. the day before yesterday, when the factory was being auctioned, President Wang sent an urgent telegram to Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of Shanghai, to advise HSBC Bank to stop the auction. Although it was too late, Mayor Wu still sent Secretary-General Yu Hongjun to HSBC Bank to persuade them. Due to the lateness of the hour, a detailed discussion could not be held. At 10:30 a.m. yesterday, Yu visited Mr. Hechman (A.S. Hechman), the chief manager of the bank. It is said that his attitude was still good, and he only said that the auction had already taken place. If the Chinese side has any solutions, they can discuss them further.

The Ministry of Industry Responded by Telegram, Applying the Civil Code. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and the Shanghai Local Association have received and understood the telegram. Since the debtor is Chinese, the procedures of Article 873 of the Civil Code should apply. The association etc. can directly request the Shanghai Municipal Government to negotiate. (Signed) Ministry of Industry. According to a reporter from the New Voice News Agency, Article 873 of the Civil Code, mentioned in the telegram, reads as follows: If the mortgagee has not been repaid after the debt has reached the due date for repayment, he may petition the court to auction the mortgaged property and receive repayment from the proceeds of the sale. An agreement that the ownership of the mortgaged property shall be transferred to the mortgagee when the debt has reached the due date for repayment and has not been repaid is invalid.

The Huayin Consortium Decided to Appeal. According to the Central News Agency, in addition to HSBC Bank, Shenxin No. 7 Factory also borrowed from a consortium of Chinese banks, including China Bank, Shanghai Bank, and other Huichang banks. This time, HSBC Bank resolutely and independently carried out the auction of the factory. The consortium jointly appointed representatives from China Bank and Shanghai Bank to submit an application to the First Special District Court for a preliminary attachment order. Now that HSBC Bank has resolutely carried out the auction, it is actually illegal. Therefore, China Bank and Shanghai Bank have decided to file an appeal, and the court will also handle the matter in accordance with the law to seek fairness. Furthermore, Lawyer Guo Shouyi of Shenxin Textile Company also issued an urgent notice yesterday morning, denying that the auction had obtained legal ownership.

The Composition of the Second Creditor Group. Yesterday, a Central News Agency reporter visited the person in charge of the China Bank representative of the second creditor. According to him, this consortium was established in June 1934, consisting of China Bank, Shanghai Bank, and thirteen Huichang banks, including Zhixiang, Qingcheng, Henglong, Qingda, Rongkang, Henglai, Zifeng, Dingkang, Heping, Huicheng, Futai, Baofeng, and Xinkang. At that time, the financial community was determined to use its strength to assist our critically endangered industrial sector. Rong Zongjing, the general manager of Shenxin Textile Company, in order to maintain various industries, mortgaged several yarn factories and other properties worth more than 10 million yuan to the consortium for a loan of 2.8 million yuan (of which the Huichang banks accounted for 320,000 yuan). Among the above-mentioned mortgaged properties, Shenxin No. 7 Factory was also one of them. At that time, HSBC Bank also acknowledged that this consortium was the second creditor. Now, it has suddenly changed its attitude, only considering its own interests and disregarding the law and human sentiment, and handed it over to the auction house for auction at a very low bid price. It is deeply regrettable. At present, lawyers from both sides are responsible for exchanging opinions to seek a solution. If it is still impossible to resolve, we can only seek legal protection, and people from all walks of life in our country will surely rise up to support us.

The Factory Association Held a Meeting and Sent Telegrams of Appeal. According to the Guowen News Agency, the China Cotton Mill Owners Association held an extraordinary executive committee meeting at 3 p.m. yesterday because HSBC Bank illegally auctioned the Shanghai Shenxin No. 7 Factory. Fifteen committee members attended, chaired by Guo Shun. The following resolutions were made: (1) To organize a sub-committee to study the measures, and immediately appoint Guo Shun, Nie Lusheng, and Liu Mengjing as members. (2) To send telegrams to Chairman Jiang in Wuchang, the Central Party Headquarters in Nanjing, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and the Shanghai Municipal Government, requesting them to take immediate measures to save the situation. (Remainder omitted.) The meeting adjourned at 5:30 p.m. Yesterday, the association sent telegrams to the government authorities based on the motion, saying: Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, President Wang of the Executive Yuan, Minister Wang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, Minister Wang of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, Commander-in-Chief Jiang of the Wuchang Headquarters, and Mayor Wu of the Shanghai Municipal Government, respectfully reviewed. The Shanghai Shenxin No. 7 Factory was illegally auctioned by the British HSBC Bank on the 26th of this month, disregarding the preliminary attachment ruling of the Shanghai Special District Local Court, which is detrimental to the dignity of the country and concerns the future of the national cotton textile industry. The impact is enormous. It is also heard that foreign businessmen intend to take over the factory's property, which may lead to serious problems. We are panicking and earnestly request you to quickly take measures to stop it, so as to protect national rights and maintain industry. Respectfully, China Cotton Mill Owners Association, Qin.

The Financial Community Expressed Deep Regret. A Central News Agency reporter also interviewed a prominent figure in the financial community. According to him, HSBC Bank's audacious auction of Shenxin No. 7 Factory is a concrete manifestation of capitalist countries destroying national industry. What is most regrettable is that it disregards the feelings of colleagues and the commercial customs and social and economic conditions of the location of the bank. Last year, HSBC was once in a difficult situation. Although Chinese banks have long been oppressed by foreign banks, in order to coexist and prosper with colleagues, the Four Banks Joint Savings Society and China Bank jointly provided a huge sum of 5 million yuan. Kicking someone when they are down is something that our national morality despises. Moreover, there is more than one Chinese industry mortgaged to foreign banks. If this trend continues, those who are unable to repay on time due to special reasons will be handed over to the auction house for auction one by one, and there will be no such thing as commercial morality. If this matter is not rectified, then the Chinese people will inevitably be wary of foreign banks and change their original intentions. As for the fact that no Chinese competed during the auction, it has aroused astonishment among social人士. However, the preliminary attachment of Shenxin No. 7 Factory is well known, which is enough to show that Chinese businessmen respect the law. No one will regard this easily obtainable huge profit as worthless, because 2.25 million yuan is not an insignificant amount.

The Industrial Federation Sent an Urgent Telegram. According to the Shiye News Agency, the China General Chamber of Industry held an emergency meeting of all members at the Yiyou Society on Sanma Road at 4 p.m. yesterday to discuss remedial measures. Twelve people attended, including Hu Xiyuan, Guo Shun, Wu Yunshu, Qian Chengxu, Cai Shengbai, and Wang Yaochen. Guo Shun chaired the meeting. It was unanimously resolved to oppose HSBC Bank's illegal auction and to send an urgent telegram to the government requesting prompt relief. The original telegram said: Nanjing National Government, Executive Yuan, Ministry of Judicial Administration, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Industry, respectfully reviewed. Shenxin No. 7 Factory was illegally auctioned by HSBC Bank, infringing on China's legal rights and destroying our national industry. (1) The mortgagee, China Bank and Shanghai Bank, has already requested the local court to implement preliminary attachment on the property, and has also notified the British Consulate for reference. However, HSBC ignored everything and disregarded China's legal rights. This is the most serious case. Regarding this matter, the government should come forward to negotiate with the position of the state, so as to make HSBC stop and hand over the property to the buyer, and HSBC should be responsible for its losses. (2) To take a step back, that is, to handle it in accordance with the legal procedures of various countries. The debtor should be notified 20 hours before the auction to allow them to make final preparations. Today, HSBC did not do this, and even according to the laws of that country, it should be subject to illegal punishment. We request the government to take urgent steps and ask the British Shanghai Court to immediately issue an injunction to stop HSBC from exercising its property rights. Respectfully, China General Chamber of Industry, Gan.

Various Sectors Met to Discuss Assistance Measures. According to the Dagong News Agency, the National Goods Factory Association held a reception for all sectors at the Atlantic Western Restaurant at 6 p.m. yesterday to discuss assistance measures. More than 60 representatives from more than 30 groups, including the China General Chamber of Industry, the Shanghai Citizens Advocating National Goods Association, the China National Goods Maintenance Association, the General Labor Union, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Citizens' Union, and the China National Products Factory Association, including Qian Chengxu, Wu Zhihao, and Zhu Xuefan, attended. Chairman Zhang Zilian reported, roughly saying that since the Shenxin Textile Company's No. 7 Factory was illegally auctioned to a Japanese company by HSBC Bank at the lowest price of 2.25 million yuan, the government and all sectors of society have been arguing on the basis of reason. All the employees of the factory, with the mentality of "if the lips are gone, the teeth will be cold," and the livelihoods of more than 10,000 employees, are about to fall into a desperate situation. At this time of social depression, imperialism is wantonly exerting its toxic flames of economic aggression and oppression, destroying industry, which is an unprecedented painful history for our country's industrial sector. Today, we are hosting representatives from all sectors to discuss assistance measures to maintain our country's industry.

Shenxin Representative Reported on the Process. Sun Zhencheng, a representative of Shenxin Factory, reported on the process, saying that Shenxin No. 7 Factory was reorganized from the Oriental Yarn Factory, which was purchased from British businessmen by Mr. Rong Zongjing and others in 1930. Since then, Mr. Rong has worked hard to plan, add spindles, improve materials, and spared no effort in construction, recovering rights and interests for the country and stabilizing the livelihoods of employees, which is well known to everyone. The value of fixed assets such as land, buildings, and machinery in the entire factory has reached more than 7 million yuan. In order to circulate national turnover, a loan of 2 million yuan was mortgaged to the British HSBC Bank. Interest payments totaling more than 1 million yuan have been paid over the years without interruption. Last year, the price of cotton was high and the price of yarn was low, and foreign goods were dumped fiercely. Affected by the economic depression, a loan of 2.8 million yuan was borrowed from China Bank and Shanghai Bank. Recently, a notice of催償 from HSBC Bank was received, and several negotiations were made, but they were rejected. Subsequently, funds were raised to redeem the factory and to pay all the interest. When consulting, the bank refused to accept the interest and, without legal procedures, entrusted Lussier and Moore Auction House to reduce the price of the factory's entire property to 2.25 million yuan and illegally auction it. Before the auction was held, the factory had entrusted Lawyer Guo Shouyi to publish an advertisement opposing the illegal auction. Another creditor of the factory, China Bank and Shanghai Bank, had already submitted an application to the Shanghai First Special District Court to execute a preliminary attachment on the factory's property. Without the approval of our court, no one may arbitrarily or in any way deal with the property. It was also heard that the court had sent personnel to the British Consulate to request that the auction be stopped. However, the bank still went its own way, using high-pressure tactics, and specially instructed Lussier and Moore Auction House to execute the illegal auction. The factory currently has more than 52,000 spindles, more than 8,000 thread spindles, and more than 440 looms. The value of the property, including land and buildings, is more than 5 million yuan. One day, it was illegally reduced in price and auctioned by the bank. Not only did the factory suffer unlimited damage, but also more than 4,000 employees in the entire factory are in danger of losing their jobs. Industry is the lifeline of people's livelihood, and justice is the prestige of the country. Looking at the bank's blatant disregard for the behavior, what is it like to destroy our country's industry? What is it like to undermine our country's justice? Its intention is obvious. Our factory is a member of the National Goods Factory Association. I am honored to report on the process at the request of Chairman Zhang. I hope you will give me your guidance. I am very grateful.

Seven Resolutions Were Made to Provide Assistance. After the representatives present spoke one after another, the assistance measures were resolved as follows: (1) The associations present will jointly submit a petition to the government, requesting the government to seriously negotiate with the British Consul regarding HSBC Bank's illegal auction of Shenxin No. 7 Factory. (2) Jointly send a letter to HSBC Bank to warn it to abide by the laws of the country where it is located. (3) Jointly send a letter to the banking and money industries to assist Shenxin and provide economic support at the end of the negotiations. (4) Elect Qian Chengxu, Zhu Xuefan, Lu Xingzhuang, Zhu Wenqi, Zhang Zilian, Wang Jiean, and Chen Binghui to petition the municipal government. (5) Telegraph the government to allocate 2.25 million yuan from the unified cotton tax to repay HSBC. If the goal cannot be achieved, the deduction will be made by each factory. (6) Appoint Tao Leqin, Ren Jinpin, Li Cishan, Qin Daishi, and Cao Zhigong to draft the telegram. (7) A meeting will be held tomorrow (today) at 10 a.m. at the Factory Association on Sanma Road to discuss the implementation measures.

Emergency Meeting of National Manufacturers. The Shanghai China National Products Manufacturers Association, in view of the fact that the British HSBC Bank blatantly auctioned Shenxin Yarn Factory's No. 7 Factory regardless of everything, convened a temporary emergency meeting at 9 a.m. yesterday. More than ten committee members attended, including Wang Hanqiang, Liu Zhongying, Jin Weixuan, and Chen Binghui. Secretary Zhou Zhaolin and Chairman Liu Zhongying attended as observers. Xu Chengde took the minutes. They discussed how to assist and provide relief in the case of the British HSBC Bank's blatant auction of Shenxin No. 7 Factory regardless of everything. The following resolutions were made: (1) To telegraph the central government, the Executive Yuan, and the ministries of industry, foreign affairs, and finance to provide as much relief and negotiation as possible. (2) To notify national manufacturers throughout the city to sever ties with foreign banks from now on (measures to be determined separately) and to send letters to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce and the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce to instruct them to proceed accordingly. (3) To send personnel to慰問 Rong Zongjing, the general manager of Shenxin Yarn Factory, and all colleagues of Shenxin No. 7 Factory. The National Products Manufacturers Association sent a letter to the national manufacturers in the city based on the resolutions of the emergency meeting, saying: Dear Sirs, according to yesterday's newspaper report, we were deeply saddened to read the news that Shenxin Yarn Factory's No. 7 Factory was illegally auctioned by the British HSBC Bank. We found that Shenxin Yarn Factory's No. 7 Factory, due to the lack of economic turnover, had previously mortgaged the entire property to the British HSBC Bank, which is an inevitable remedy in the midst of this widespread depression and the decline of industry and commerce. Now, the bank does not take the circulation of finance and serving the community as its responsibility, but uses the excuse that the factory cannot redeem the mortgage on time, and blatantly disregards everything, disposing of the factory's huge property worth 5 million yuan without the consent of the property owner, and unilaterally announces the auction. As a result, it was auctioned to a Japanese company for the lowest price of 2.25 million yuan. It can be seen that foreign banks rely on their imperialist economic aggression and blatantly destroy our country's industry. In addition to reporting to the central government and sending letters to all sectors to provide as much relief and negotiation as possible and make a strong resistance, we have also resolved to notify national goods manufacturers throughout the city to sever ties with foreign banks from now on. All national goods merchants must take the lead and earnestly implement this measure. We are sending this letter to you for your information and implementation. We are deeply grateful.

Rong Expressed Extreme Pain. A Central News Agency reporter also met with Rong Zongjing, the general manager of Shenxin Company, at his private residence. In addition to expressing his pain, Rong said that he was still determined to revitalize the industry he had worked so hard to build all his life with his inherent ambition. Rong also said that HSBC's blatant auction of Shenxin No. 7 Factory was a deliberate attempt to destroy our country's industry. I am determined to resist to the end. I only hope that the government authorities and those who care about and love our country's industrial sector will jointly provide practical assistance and fair public opinion to avoid being wiped out by HSBC. Shenxin No. 7 Factory is still working as usual, pending the court's disposal.

A Letter Was Sent to the Bar Association for Discussion. Shenxin Textile Company sent a letter to the Shanghai Bar Association yesterday, saying: Dear Sirs, Shenxin No. 7 Factory of our company previously mortgaged its factory buildings, land, machinery, etc., worth more than 5 million yuan, to HSBC Bank for a loan of 2 million yuan. Later, due to the impact of the economic depression, the difficulties reached the extreme, resulting in the inability to repay the mortgage on time. In addition to entrusting Lawyer Guo Shouyi to publish advertisements and oppose the auction, we are writing to your association to request you to promptly discuss it to provide remedies. We earnestly pray. Sincerely, Shenxin Textile Company, February 27th.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Reduced Passenger Ticket Prices for the Si Hai Vessel 124

Reduced the Burden on Passengers

Only 60% of the Listed Price Is Charged

Since its launch, the newly built China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Si Hai vessel has been popular with passengers traveling to various ports in South China because of its beautiful layout, attentive service, and excellent security equipment. The price of first-class tickets from Shanghai to Shantou, Xiamen, Hong Kong, and Guangzhou was originally set at 75 yuan from Shanghai to Xiamen, 80 yuan to Shantou, 85 yuan to Hong Kong, and 95 yuan to Guangzhou. In order to give preferential treatment to passengers and reduce the burden on Chinese passengers taking the Si Hai vessel, the first-class ticket prices have been sharply reduced, so that passengers can travel at the most affordable fare and take the best seats. Shanghai to Xiamen is now reduced to 42 yuan (33 yuan less than the original price), to Shantou is reduced to 45 yuan (35 yuan less), to Hong Kong is reduced to 50 yuan (35 yuan less), and to Guangdong is reduced to 54 yuan (41 yuan less). It is cheaper than any foreign vessel on the same route. The service of the attendants is especially attentive. They do not ask passengers for any tips, which is a unique feature of the shipping industry. It is heard that in the Haili vessel, several passengers strongly gave rewards, but the attendants firmly refused to accept them. After going back and forth seven times, the passengers became angry and, as a result, deposited the money in the accounting room, and the attendants never received a penny. Currently, the company stipulates that there will be a ship leaving Shanghai for Shantou, Hong Kong, and Guangzhou every Wednesday and Saturday, and a ship leaving Shanghai for Qingdao every Saturday. The first-class room from Shanghai to Qingdao is only 40 yuan.

Pilot Cullenberg of Eurasia Crashes and Dies in Hankou Yesterday Morning 125

The company has decided to provide generous compensation according to regulations

The crashed aircraft has been repaired and flown to Hankou

The Eurasia Aviation Corporation's No. 3 aircraft, flying the Guangzhou (Canton) line, crashed in Yichang County, on the border of Hunan and Hubei provinces, on the 21st due to fog. The German pilot, Cullenberg, suffered a leg injury. The company dispatched No. 8 aircraft to transport him to Hankou for hospital treatment. At the time, the Shanghai head office was informed that Mr. Cullenberg's leg injury was not serious. Nevertheless, the company prepared to send Dr. Nol, a German doctor, to Hankou on the company's large aircraft yesterday morning for a medical examination. However, just as the aircraft was about to depart from Shanghai, the company suddenly received a telegram from Hankou reporting that Mr. Cullenberg's condition had suddenly deteriorated and he had died at 9:00 AM yesterday. The company then notified Dr. Nol to cancel his flight to Hankou. According to the company's spokesperson, speaking to a Sin Sin News Agency reporter, regarding the handling of Mr. Cullenberg's funeral arrangements, the company will act in accordance with the driver's contract and provide generous compensation according to regulations. Mr. Cullenberg's family, including his wife and two daughters, originally resided in Hankou. Mr. Cullenberg himself had taken out life insurance with the German Royal Insurance Company. As for the crashed No. 3 aircraft, it has been repaired by engineers from the company's Changsha office who rushed to the accident site. Because the damage was minimal, it was repaired a few days ago and flown to Hankou yesterday afternoon. Since the flight power was not damaged, it will resume flying the Guangzhou line.

Guantai Blocking and Closing Project 127

Kong Xiangrong Telegraphed Hu Yuanhui

Attention to Preparation and Planning Matters

Kong Xiangrong, member of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee and Director of the Labor Relief Group, recently went to the construction site to inspect the water situation and construction conditions, as well as the river bureau's collection of materials and the progress of the blocking work. Detailed guidance plans were given regarding the various matters to be noted during the blocking, and they have been handed over to Hu Yuanhui, Director of the Construction Department of Hebei Province, to forward to the river bureau for compliance and strict supervision to accelerate progress. The original telegram and attached list of matters to be noted are recorded below:

Strict Telegram Urging: The Yellow River Flood Relief Committee's Labor Relief Group telegraphed Guantai, Hu Yuanhui, Director of the Construction Department of Hebei Province: (Omissions) Investigating the Guantai blocking project, the relationship is important. Since this group was ordered to supervise the progress of the Yellow River River Bureau in the province, telegrams have been repeatedly sent urging the rush to estimate the budget. From last autumn until the beginning of winter, reports were delayed. Considering that the weather was getting cold at that time, and fearing that the freezing ground would affect the work, I had no choice but to telegraph the bureau on November 5 of last year, setting a deadline of three days to estimate and send detailed estimates of each mouth and blocking. At the same time, I personally went to the construction site to inspect and wait, and the estimate was finally submitted after investigation. I then contracted with the Yellow Benefit Association to approve and order compliance, and immediately began to supervise the bureau to purchase materials, rush to hire box boats, transport iron anchors, recruit workers, and also dispatched personnel to the construction site to assist in case of emergency, and allocated funds from time to time to provide a steady stream of supplies. On November 17 of last year, I telegraphed the bureau, setting a deadline of one month to complete the blocking, and on the 20th of the same month, I set a deadline of two weeks to transport all materials for preparation, so as to avoid temporary panic, suspension of work while waiting for materials, and delaying important work. Telegrams were exchanged frequently, without a day of rest. The original plan was to rush to block and close the gap before the winter solstice (December 22) according to the original planned steps. The bureau also replied on December 13, stating that it had strictly urged efforts to work and block in time, so as not to delay the work. Unexpectedly, as of December 18, although 781 meters of the mouth had been occupied, only 64 meters remained. At that time, the water was calm, which was a good time to rush to block, but because the jute ordered by the bureau's supervisor, He Du Xiu, was far away in Jining and could not be obtained, the great opportunity to block and lower the water level before the winter solstice was lost. After that, either the straw was missing, or the jute was missing, and the straw and jute could not be delivered to the work site in large quantities at the same time. Day after day, the water level gradually rose, and the mouth became deeper and deeper. The work situation deteriorated, and the original estimated materials were used up for emergency protection, resulting in insufficient application of the original work funds. In this extremely difficult situation, Rong discussed relief measures at the work site and submitted a request to this association to allocate relief from the remaining funds of the Fenglou blocking project last year, and also added 3 million catties of straw, 50,000 catties of jute, and 30,000 green bricks, and increased personnel to assist in hiring boats for transportation and intensify work to make up for the situation in many ways, setting a deadline of two weeks to be responsible for blocking and closing the gap. The bureau also stated in the case of applying for additional external engineering fees on December 24 that the various materials should be the responsibility of the bureau to actively purchase and transport, purchasing all of them within 12 days, and aiming to close the gap within 14 days. According to the original presentation, the materials should be transported by January 5 of this year, and the blocking should begin on the 7th. Considering the urgency of closing the gap and the importance of materials, which must be fully prepared to meet the emergency needs and provide resources for rushing to block, this group strictly telegraphed to urge on December 28 of last year, and on the 29th, ordered the concentration of employees to rush to build side dams. However, on January 3 of this year, the resident inspectors of this group reported that the bureau's straw, green bricks, jute, etc. were all insufficient. After strict urging, they still failed to transport all the materials on time, and the river water was falling on the 7th. The water depth in front of the east and west dams was only a little over 8 meters. If the blocking could have been carried out as scheduled, it would have been closed long ago. Those who urged kept urging, and those who delayed kept delaying, and this best opportunity was missed again. It is extremely regrettable to say. By the 17th of the same month, the entire river was flowing with ice, and the continued supply of materials was stopped again. It was found that on February 3 of this year, the water level had become stable, and the water depth of the two dams was only over 8 meters. However, due to the bureau's repeated inconsistencies between words and deeds, and the delay in transporting materials, the blocking could not be carried out. As of the end of last year of the abolished calendar, three good opportunities for blocking and closing the gap had been lost. On February 5 of this year, this group, together with the Yellow Benefit Association and your Director, discussed the method of blocking and closing the gap. Jute bags, green bricks, lead wire box boats, iron anchors, etc., were all limited to being prepared and delivered to the work site by the evening of the 11th of this month, and construction would begin on the 11th, occupation would begin on the 15th, and closure would be achieved on the 23rd and 24th. Now that only a few days remain, the bureau's straw and other items are again overdue. According to reports, today's water situation is turning better to the south. The 2 million catties of straw and 100,000 green bricks prepared by this group have arrived at the work site one after another. The 300 cubic meters of stone have also been purchased and transported from Gongyi. 50,000 jute bags have been ordered in Shanghai according to instructions and negotiated to use the original vehicles for direct transportation, without changing vehicles along the way. The joint transportation method will be fully delivered to the work site within days. Fearing that the urgent use is too urgent, we have also negotiated with the Henan River Bureau to borrow 10,000 jute bags. Tomorrow, after the formalities of the Henan Provincial Government's approval and handover to the River Bureau, they can be transported. We also plan to negotiate with the Henan River Bureau to borrow 100 to 200 cubic meters of stone for emergency needs. In addition to those who have been dispatched, more personnel will be added to the two dams to supervise and assist in the work. In addition, as discussed in person at the work site yesterday, the Director will send personnel to Hankou to purchase and transport 50,000 jute bags, and Shi Yun Gong will provide emergency supplies. I don't know if they have been purchased and shipped on time. I hope they will be delivered on time to avoid delays. As for the additional yellow materials, reed mats, cattail bags, wooden stakes, jute, etc. requested by the River Bureau, the amount of money needed is not much, and the River Bureau should immediately handle them according to the amount received. The various materials requested by the River Bureau have been planned and collected in advance. As for the item of earth resistance and earth filling, not only funds are needed for handling, but also preparations should be made in advance in detail. Please allocate funds nearby and guide the progress immediately. If orderly and systematic steps can be taken, and the blocking can be carried out according to the established plan, it will not be difficult to complete it in one breath. The various items that should be noted during the blocking are listed separately below. Please forward them to the River Bureau for information, so as to be comprehensive, so that we can see the success early and rejoice together. Special telegram for inspection, and I hope you will strictly supervise it. Rong has prepared the urgently needed materials and will return to the work site tomorrow. I know and hear together.

Instruction Plan: Matters to be noted in the preparation and planning of the Guantai Blocking and Closing Project: (1) It is found that the Guantai project has repeatedly failed to carry out blocking as scheduled due to the lack of materials in the River Bureau. Now that the materials have been prepared, the progress of blocking and closing the gap must be properly planned and handled in advance to avoid temporary panic. The first question to be determined now is whether to rush to build the counter cabinet first and then occupy, or to occupy first and then rush to build the counter cabinet. If the counter cabinet is rushed first, the back river of the two dams will be scoured, which will definitely not be able to catch up in a short time. It is deeply felt that the occupation will be difficult and slow. Moreover, the current value of water falling is a pity to lose the opportunity. If the occupation is advanced and the counter cabinet is rushed later, the isolated occupation will be tightened and the scouring will be deepened, which is even more dangerous. Although the back filling cabinet after connecting to the old occupation is relatively easy to handle, it is still not easy to advance with the new advance occupation and the back filling cabinet, because the mouth is narrow, the water flow is more rapid, and the swirling flow is still inevitable. Which one should be first and which one should be later should be considered early. (2) The most important thing when closing the gap is earthwork. The east dam is 1,500 feet long, and the west dam is also 1,000 feet long. There is no soil to be taken from the earth fields on both sides. It is estimated that when closing the gap, the soil in the middle earth cabinet is temporarily calculated as 10 feet long, 15 feet wide, and 50 feet high, which requires about 750 cubic feet. The east dam soil truck travels three miles back and forth, and the west dam soil truck is no less than two miles. According to the previous soil pushing achievements, it is estimated that each truck can extract 2 points of soil per day. How many trucks are needed each day for each dam to be sufficient? Moreover, the dam surface is not wide, how many soil trucks can it accommodate, and the distribution of truck roads are all important issues. If there are 300 soil trucks per dam per day, a total of 120 cubic feet of dam work can be done per day (losses are not yet counted). It takes 6-7 days to fill the earth cabinet. Can Jinmen's occupation be relied on for a long time? This is a very big problem and should be paid special attention to. Moreover, the earth filling behind the side dam is not easy to handle. In this situation, whether it is to rush to build the cabinet and then occupy, or to advance the occupation and rush to build the counter cabinet, the soil truck cannot rush urgently, and it is necessary to quickly purchase a large amount of jute bags to hold soil instead of rushing to handle it temporarily. As for the soil in the earth cabinet, calculated at 70 bags per cubic foot, about 50,000 bags are needed. If cloth bags are used instead, it is feared that three times as many will be needed, even small jute bags must be doubled. This kind of jute bag must be made early, stored near the doorway for backup supply, which is extremely important and cannot be slightly ignored. It is more necessary to delineate the truck road to avoid soil accumulation and crowding, or to store more earth oxen for temporary use, because the earth cabinet is not all made of jute bag soil. As for the place where the earth is pushed after the side dam of the mouth, because the scouring is too deep, it is not easy to fill and help with soil. It is necessary to rush to fill with bag soil. The number of this item of jute bags is not small, and it must be carefully calculated in advance. The truck route, the issuing and receiving of soil tickets, the exchange of cash, and the preparation of soil trucks, and the allocation of supervisory officers and yamen runners should all be considered in advance and properly planned and distributed. The difficulty of advancing the earth filing after all the earth cabinets are advanced before and after the closing is as described above, but only before the earth cabinet has not been filled under Jinmen's occupation, the river bottom is thinly silted, and it is feared that the undercurrent will attack the positive dam foot sweep. It is necessary to take emergency protection and slowly advance the earth resistance to avoid mistakes. The material for protection is to first throw jute bags, and then use crude stones, or use lead jute cages to cage stones and throw them into a slope, one is to avoid the danger of large flows on the top, and the other is to protect the broom feet from scouring again. Especially for the throwing protection of crude stones, it must be extra careful to avoid the flow into the mouth and hinder the occupation. This item of jute bags does not expect how much each is needed, and must be purchased in advance, transported in unity, and properly packed for use. This layer is extremely important and cannot be ignored. It should also be planned and handled properly at the same time. (4) It is found that the east dam is 1,500 feet long, and the early occupation made is more than two-thirds. The broom height water surface is only 2 meters low, and the dam width is wider than the deep water occupation, and the rest are 2 to 2.5 feet. The occupation body is short and weak, and the back earthwork is also weak. After the mouth is closed, the water level rises, or the big river water rises, and the flow directly tends to the east dam. The newly silted sand is inevitable to seep and brush the broom, and should be carefully investigated to prevent potential pitfalls. It is appropriate to throw protection for the welcoming flow top punch with jute bag crude stone brick cages. The bay protruding place is suitable for the flow rushing out of the sand beach on the west bank. More crude stones should be thrown to prevent the flow from leaning against the broom and avoid scouring. And investigate other places where the slip shoots, and throw protection in advance in this way, which is more stable. Where the dam body is low and thin, the soil should also be appropriately increased to increase the pressure and reduce seepage and brushing. The amount of jute bag crude stone needed should be calculated early. At this time, special attention should be paid to the broom that the east dam advances and borders, and its river bottom. The broom eyes should be free of seepage, and the west dam's broom should be carefully repaired when it has been subsided repeatedly, without perfunctory. Before closing the gap, increase the throwing of protective feet bricks, stones, and jute bags to prevent seepage. (5) According to recent reports from resident inspectors, the river flows south, and the sand beach is exposed in front of the mouth near the river. The river water is falling, and the water is shallow where the river mouth branches, and the flow is not wide. If willows can be dropped to form a dam or sign piles can be sunk to reduce the mouth flow, personnel should be sent to investigate the terrain and river situation and handle it carefully. This layer is very important and should be paid special attention to. (6) It is only a little over a month away from Taofan. After the Guantai closing, it seems that it will not be possible to complete the closing of mouths such as Jiugu Road in a very short time. The Zizhen that connects the east and west dams of Guantai is about 2 meters high from the current water surface. The trench site is low and the trench body is thin. Can it resist water? In addition, the various string ditches blocked below Guantai must be increased at the same time, or choose to do protective eaves broom to avoid digging wells when thirsty and delaying the completed work. This should also be paid special attention to. In addition, it is especially important to assign working personnel in advance to their respective duties, and it is more necessary to unite in spirit and work hard to serve, with the determination to block the gap, forge ahead bravely, be of one mind and cooperate, divide the work and cooperate, and achieve success. This is also in the guidance of the chief officer in charge, and colleagues do their best to be responsible. Then the great success will be achieved in no time, and the lives and property of millions of people will be relied upon. Rong is not talented, and is willing to follow in the footsteps of the gentlemen to encourage people to encourage themselves. Attached by Kong Xiangrong, Director of the Labor Relief Group.

The China-America Tobacco Company started the Standard Great Man Election Scholarship in Chinese history on September 1st last year. There was a unanimous response from all over the country. More than 100,000 students from all levels of schools in the city participated. The results were announced on January 31st of this year.
