Decline of Northeast Culture: Current Situation of Slave Education in Liaoning and Jilin 172

Dalian Establishes Industrial School but Implementation Difficult Due to Lack of Funds

Jilin's Funding Becomes Increasingly Tight, School Buildings Collapse, and Five Schools Merge

(Northeast News Agency) Northeast education is declining due to the continuous cultural aggression of the Japanese. Therefore, Northeast youth today not only suffer from the pain of being out of school but also from the harm of Japanese anesthetic education. After receiving their slavish training, their ambition to save our motherland and their impression of the motherland gradually fade away. In this environment, the future of Northeast youth is truly dangerous and heartbreaking. The recent education situation in Liaoning and Jilin provinces is described below:

Liaoning (1) (Fengcheng County News) Sun Xiaolin, the president of the Fengcheng Education Association, has resigned because the violent Japanese forced him to implement slave education too excessively, which went against his conscience. The deputy president, Yuan Qinghe, has been temporarily appointed by the puppet county government to act as president. However, the term of office of the president and vice president of the association is about to expire, so the puppet county government used this reason to request approval from the puppet Fengtian Education Association to elect the president and vice president in advance. The association has now notified the principals and educators of all schools in Fengcheng County that they must be present to vote when the time comes. (2) He Qintang, the director of the puppet education bureau of Fengcheng County, is now trying to please the Japanese and show his efforts to promote slave education as the winter vacation ends and school is about to start. He is holding an educational conference at the site of the County No. 4 Elementary School, gathering principals of various county, district, village, and private schools. The puppet education bureau is actively preparing, and the principals of various schools have reported one after another. When the conference is held, the Japanese council officer will be invited to give guidance and instructions. (3) The Japanese authorities in Dalian City intend to win over the hearts of the people of the Northeast and implement slave education, so they plan to establish the Second Industrial School in Dalian. The construction cost is 150,000 yuan. The Japanese are using a "benevolent" policy, forcing the three chambers of commerce in Dalian to raise the funds. The three chambers of commerce held separate meetings to discuss the matter. Because the amount of 150,000 yuan was too large, they politely declined. Therefore, the mayor of Dalian criticized the associations for not being enthusiastic about public welfare and not being able to promote education. Therefore, in recent days, joint meetings of the boards of directors and presidents of the chambers of commerce and meetings of city councilors have been held to discuss why Dalian is urgently ordering the chambers of commerce to bear such a large sum of money and whether this urgent measure is inappropriate. In the end, the approval of raising funds was not passed.

Jilin (1) (Jilin News) Zhang Xiaozhai, the director of the puppet education department of Jilin Province, followed the orders of the Japanese after the implementation of the puppet new provincial system and abolished the original school names of the affiliated secondary schools, that is, the "number" of the previous schools, and implemented the new system, uniformly prefixing the school name with the name of the place to distinguish them and show uniformity. The puppet department has now completed the renaming of the various provincial-run coeducational secondary schools. The former Provincial No. 1 Normal School was renamed Jilin Provincial Normal School, the former Jilin Provincial No. 1 Engineering School was renamed Jilin Provincial Engineering Middle School, the former Jilin Provincial No. 2 Normal School was renamed Changchun Normal School, the former Jilin Provincial Women's Normal School was renamed Jilin Provincial Jilin Two-Level Women's Normal School, the former Jilin Provincial No. 1 Middle School was renamed Jilin Provincial Jilin Two-Level Middle School, the former Jilin Provincial No. 2 Middle School was renamed Jilin Provincial Changchun Junior Middle School, the former Jilin Provincial No. 5 Middle School was renamed Jilin Provincial Jilin Junior Middle School, and the former Jilin Provincial Women's Middle School was renamed Jilin Provincial Jilin Junior Women's Middle School. (2) The Provincial Jilin Normal School (No. 1 Normal School) in the East Suburb of Jilin Province is now facing the problem that its original school buildings are mostly dilapidated and difficult to support due to years of disrepair. If this continues, it is feared that there will be danger. Moreover, the puppet education department cannot allocate funds for construction and repair due to financial difficulties. It is planned to move the entire school to the old site of the police department outside Deshengmen to avoid unexpected dangers. Preparations for the relocation have begun in order to start school as soon as possible. This shows the puppet education authorities' financial difficulties and their disregard for the lives of students. (3) The Jilin Municipal Middle School on Beida Street in Jilin Province has been approved by the puppet municipal preparatory office and received by the puppet provincial government for management due to financial difficulties. Jiangsu Province Rover Scout Enlistment Standards and Training Principles 177

The Jiangsu Provincial Conference on Discussion of Boy Scout and Rover Scout Affairs has completed discussions on various proposals. The enlistment standards and training principles for Rover Scouts are stipulated as follows:

Enlistment Standards Formal members must be senior Boy Scouts who are 18 years old or older and have completed five or more specialized subjects and passed the examination, or who have passed the preparatory member examination. Preparatory members must be senior Boy Scouts who are 17 years old or older but under 18 years old, or who are 18 years old or older and have a special interest in Boy Scouting.

Training Principles (1) Leading children, training Boy Scouts and Cub Scouts, and helping poor children who have dropped out of school. (2) Military common sense, military training, battlefield service, etc. (3) Fire protection, first aid, public health, family work, and social relief undertakings. (4) Emphasizing the practice of oaths, regulations, and new life. (5) Traveling, camping, sports, swimming, Chinese martial arts, equestrian archery, calisthenics, etc. (6) Driving cars, trams, and radio communications, etc. (7) Detective science, such as police detectives, etc. (8) Natural phenomena, such as plants, animals, stars, and climate, etc. (9) Civic training, major domestic and foreign events, political and economic conditions. (10) Personal self-study, reading books and newspapers, keeping diaries, etc.

Clothing Style The clothing style, color, and quality of supplies are completely the same as those of Boy Scouts, but the hat uses a flat brim, and the scarf or tie uses green. The badge style needs to be requested from each county to solicit designs, and then decided.

Cub Scout Oath The Cub Scout oath, regulations, and motto have been stipulated: (Oath) I am willing to be a loyal citizen, and two, to abide by the Cub Scout regulations. (Regulations) One, obey, two, help others. (Motto) Strive.

Developing the Northwest Association Encourages University Students to Travel to the Northwest 185

The Northwest Territory is Vast, Making Recognition Difficult Without Personal Visits

Please Urge Students to Take More Trips to the Northwest

Chen Lifu, Chairman of the Developing the Northwest Association, recently sent letters to various universities, stating that since the September 18th National Crisis, government authorities and people from all walks of life have regarded the development of the Northwest as an essential plan for the country today. However, the Northwest territory is vast, and the social situation is complex, making thorough understanding difficult without personally visiting the region. In recent years, many people have gone to the Northwest for on-the-spot investigations or sightseeing tours, but this endeavor is rarely seen among young students. In fact, the Northwest is the birthplace of Chinese culture, with simple folk customs, abundant products, famous historical sites everywhere, and unique scenery no less impressive than that of the Southeast. Moreover, the local area has been peaceful recently, the Longhai Railway has been extended to Xi'an, and highways in various provinces have gradually developed, making transportation very convenient. If young students take advantage of their holidays to organize groups for sightseeing tours, they can not only broaden their personal horizons but also shift social attitudes. It is hoped that your esteemed Principal will encourage students to take more trips to the Northwest, so that they can inform the people of the country with their research findings, or use a particular Northwest issue as material for their university graduation thesis. If the trend catches on and the whole country is stirred up, the future prosperity of the Northwest will be greatly contributed to.

The Foreign Exchange Market Continues to Ease, and the Gold Market, Although Rising, Still Falls

New Low Price of 872 Yuan, Resulting in a Slight Drop of Two Dimes

The gold market trend is extremely weak, and the decline is endless. Only when there are rumors of the Central Bank opening for cash can the buyers become active, and the market can rebound in the middle. However, the banks' selling appetite is extremely strong, the exchange market lacks maintenance, and hedging takes the opportunity to sell off. People's hearts are inherently fearful, and the chips have been reduced to more than 18,000. The shorts are fearless, and the buyers are at a loss. A new low price of 872 yuan has been created. It is found that at the beginning of the morning, although the overseas gold markets in England and the United States rose, they did not rise much. London raw gold fell by three pence, and the off-site pre-market trading opened at 73.4 yuan. Taking advantage of the low price, there was a sudden short covering, and the price gradually rose. The Central Bank's listing was announced, and both the British and American markets were flat, and the customs gold unit fell by three cents. The standard gold price was 933 yuan and eight dimes, which had no impact. The morning opening was high. Although it was slightly flat and tired after opening, it broke through the 80 yuan mark due to large buyers entering the market. The exchange market tightened, and rumors spread that the Central Bank was opening for cash, and the price rose once. However, because the Bank of Japan continued to push out, and it was known in advance that the HSBC listing would rise again, the price gradually fell back. Although there was hovering, once the 80 yuan mark was broken, the buying interest decreased again. The banks pushed out again and again, and the exchange market was extremely tight. Under the hedging sell-off, the supply exceeded the demand, and it was difficult to maintain. A new low price of 872 yuan was created again, and then there was more trading. The Central Bank's listing was announced, and both British and American currencies were flat, and the customs gold unit fell by three cents. The exchange market was not greatly affected. Although the banks pushed out after opening, the psychological state of Chinese businessmen was relatively stable. After entering, although there were rumors that the Central Bank was opening for cash, the exchange market was completely unaffected. Banks continued to sell off, and Chinese businessmen, except for the Dalian Gang, were generally unenthusiastic. The Hong Kong side also had selling positions, which made it even harder at noon. The trend continued to loosen after the close. As the recession became more and more serious, banks and money houses did not dare to lend money, which severely hit the import business. The future of the exchange market is difficult to be optimistic. The noon close selling price for the near term British currency was one shilling, seven pence, and 125, and the US currency was 38.75 yuan, which was 0625 looser for the British currency and 125 harder for the US currency compared to the previous close. Chinese businessmen switched about 50,000 pounds sterling and more than 300,000 US dollars. Banks such as Macaulay, Sumitomo, Mitsui, Youli, Citibank, HSBC, etc. all pushed out. Spring and Autumn

Snippets 200

— (Yan BOGUANG)

Every spring, I always hear people in society talking about promoting new plans, how to save money, and thinking of ways to increase income and reduce expenditure. Time flies, and after the spring season has passed, they are still wasting money. At the end of the year, it's still a mess! Perhaps this is because people in society are implementing the plan of "the whole year's plan lies in spring"?

People who hesitate when encountering things often like to seek divination, ask for fortunes, measure words, and fortune-telling to point out the lost path. These people are really the biggest fools in the world, because if he can point out your maze, can't he point out his own?

In these few days, rich people are still having lavish spring wine parties, and they are very busy socializing. Poor families don't even have tree bark and grass roots to eat, and starve to death! It is precisely the silhouette of "Behind the red doors, meat and wine go to waste, while on the road lie the bones of those who have frozen to death!"

Lanterns Down Talk 201

— ZHANG Huang

According to the old custom, the 24th day of the first month is the Lantern Festival. On this day, everyone, big and small, must make tangyuan to eat, called "Lantern dumplings". Temples in various places have been erecting tower lanterns in front of them since the Lantern Festival. Some only light them for three days, but most of them, with sufficient funds, will light them continuously until this day before they are closed. At that time, the public must express a small commemoration of the date when this prayer for a good harvest and respect for the gods ended successfully—made dumplings and gathered with their families to eat, and they also sent them to relatives and friends and neighbors. In fact, isn't it just using a false name to satisfy the appetite—do you want the abdomen to appear abundant?

However, the scenery of the New Year has reached the end of its strength on the 24th day of the first month and cannot be missed; the public's atmosphere of revelry, following the fall of the lights, is also extinguished in the same way, and will never be allowed to be erected and lit again!

Nowadays, a group of people who know a little English and like to make Chinese-foreign combined language often embed "falling lights" (an English word) into their native language and say, "For example: 'His appearance is really "falling lights"!' means that this person's appearance is too bad. The meaning of this English word "falling lights" is similar to falling behind, and mixing it into the native language is full of Europeanization (?) glory. Or, let's force a metaphor for this word, as a metaphor that when the lamp falls, not only does it lose its brilliance, but it is also not suitable for the times.

The lanterns are down, the days of joy are over, but the courage of people to step up their business and work after the Lantern Festival should be like the lights on the top of the tower, towering high in the sky, shining brightly, and don't fall down soon and willingly join the ranks of "falling lights"! May everyone remember to encourage themselves with falling lights!

A Boat on a Snowy Night 202

— QING Qu

"Snow" was originally an auspicious sign of a good harvest, but the prognosticators say: If it snows in December, then the two wheat crops in the coming spring will be ripe; therefore, there is a saying: "December snow is like a quilt, spring snow is like a ghost," and also called "If you want wheat, see three white," meaning that getting snow three times is what farmers hope for most; Alas! Unexpectedly, God did not send snow in December, but it snowed several times in the spring. It is the same snow, but people's feelings about it are somewhat different.

One day, Qu Qu and his old friends, Lawyer Gu Mengfei, Huang Jun Tianbai, etc., went to the southwest countryside for business. If they went by waterway, it would be too much trouble: So, outside Ximen, they hired a small boat and a boatman named "Xixi" to go to the middle road; At this time, it was just the spring cold, and the six petals were flying. After not a few moments, it was like Baiyong Languan. Without saying to go back, the boat sailed, passing through many small bridges I do not know how many. The destination was still far away. Suddenly, I glanced at a bridge. Its area was as flat as water, like a boat could not pass through it. Hey! As we got closer, we slowly went away.

Huang Jun Tianbai held a glass and drank and chanted, and Yu couldn't help but kneaded a sentence, "The snow presses the heart of the bridge, and the two banks are wide." Because at this moment, it was already dusk, but it was all white, so the riverside was really inseparable from the earth, which was very beautiful; Yu asked Tianbai to write a couplet, and Tianbai continued the next sentence, "The wind blows the stern of the boat, a pot of spring." Everyone floated a big white; Later, Mengfei didn't speak for a while, and suddenly shouted, "Got it," saying: The word "blow" in the wind "blow" feels very inappropriate, and it should be changed to a word "return". The wind turns back, so that the wine will not be cold and lose its warmth, so it is appropriate to the word "spring". We both admire his iron-like skills, and the poetic rhythm is better than the law. We drank with a roar, and after a while, that country friend had been waiting in front of the house for a long time, and held hands to go up.

Civilization and Barbarism 203

— JIANG Mi

Little Western Paradise 204

— Written by ZHANG Henshui

Chapter 9: Failing to Compliment, Begging for Help, Being Scolded, Failing to Return, Following the Guest, Exaggerated

Although he was poor, he always had the experience of sitting in a chair, so he sat very carelessly, but he didn't expect that after sitting down, he seemed to feel that the seat board of the guest chair sank down with his butt, probably because he sat too hard, so he broke the chair. He was so scared that he held the table along and immediately sat up. Looking back, he gained a bit of knowledge. It turned out that the seat of the chair was not a wooden board, but a leaky net woven of rattan silk. In Gansu, he always sits on a soil pit. It is amazing to be able to find two or three square stools to sit on at someone else's house. This Little Western Paradise is really testing people. Guests are not allowed to be wronged by their butts when sitting on chairs, and they have come up with tricks to make people enjoy it. Thinking in his heart, showing a hesitant attitude, it was very ugly. Jia Duocai smiled and said: Your small feet, why are you still being polite with us? Just sit down. Mr. Hu put his hands behind his back and stretched down, groping for a while at the rattan net surface of the chair, and then slowly and lightly sat down. Jia Duocai sat far diagonally opposite him, looked at him, and then looked at Yueying standing on the corner of the table, thinking in his heart, I didn't expect such a mother to give birth to this wonderful daughter, is it strange? That time, Yueying sat here, and Jia Duocai couldn't bear to look at her, but today he looked at her like this again. But he also wanted to break it. If he didn't let people like him, how could he hope for help? This man surnamed Jia, as long as he met him, would stare at him with his eyes, that is to say, he had a bit of liking for him. As long as he was willing to want him, let him watch it for a while. What's the use of being shy? Eating and dressing are the most important things. Thinking like this, he didn't know how to be shy, just lowered his head slightly, and stood firmly with his hands on the table. Jia Duocai saw that although he held his face, it was still red in the white, which clearly meant that he was still quite embarrassed, which added to his charm. (144)

Royal Incense Drifting Record 205

— Originally Written by Princess DE LING, Translated by QIN Shouou

My heart to return was simply more eager than everyone else's. Although I had already gotten on the train, I was still holding a handful of cold sweat, fearing that some unexpected event would happen in these last few minutes, preventing us from escaping. But people's psychology is often very contradictory: Although I was worried and anxious on the one hand, on the other hand, I was firmly leaning against the car window, looking backwards as much as possible, hoping that something would really happen.

"Hey! Deling! The train is about to leave! You can't look behind anymore! It's very unlucky!" The Empress Dowager saw that I was looking too mesmerized, and she became unhappy in her heart, so she shouted at me very sternly. Of course, I didn't dare to ask her why it was unlucky to look back: I had to immediately turn my head and stand upright.

Just like when we came, the whistle didn't blow, and the alarm clock didn't ring. Our special train quietly rolled. Two or three hours before it started to roll, all other trains on the entire Beijing-Fengtian line were prohibited from moving; Local officials from all over had also sent people to carefully guard both sides of the track; Everything was the same as when we came. The only difference was the speed of the train. When we came, the Empress Dowager desperately ordered us to go slowly, as if the slower the better: Now, she wants it to go as fast as possible. However, even though the old man ordered this, the driver did not dare to drive at full speed and speed; Because when we set off, they had been warned very severely that there must be no violent vibrations when the car was running, and if the train was to run fast, vibration was absolutely inevitable. Therefore, in order to achieve both goals, the driver had to drive the train faster than when it came and slower than the usual passenger car. This way, it was fast, and the vibration was not very violent! Watching the trees and fields outside the car window retreat backwards like a revolving lantern, we knew that our train was indeed running much faster than before. (255)

Love and Hate (Part 2) 206

— Tao Hancui

Furthermore, Yi Yun had heard some anecdotes about him, more moving than the various romantic histories circulating about Sai Jinhua. Therefore, he was exceedingly fond of this photograph. He brought it home and hid it in his study. Whenever he sat in his study, bothered beyond relief by the noise from the old woman next door, he would take out and admire this extremely lovely photograph, using it as his only means of dispelling the annoyance.

One day, this photograph was discovered by Yi Yun's younger sister, Kezhen. She happily took it to the Yu family's parlor to show the old woman, asking if the person in the photograph was pretty. The old woman took one look and suddenly exclaimed to Kezhen, asking where this photograph came from. Kezhen said her brother bought it from a street stall. The old woman then told Kezhen that the person in the photograph was herself, remembering it was taken when she was nineteen at a photo studio on the road outside the city. This photograph was likely a reprint from that studio. However, she did not reveal that at nineteen, she was a famous courtesan in Suzhou.

Yi Yun, sitting in his study next door, heard everything the old woman said very clearly. But he never imagined that this extremely detestable old woman was actually the incarnation of Peihong, the famous beauty of the Wu Palace, whom he considered extremely lovely. Even now, when he thinks about this, he still feels confused and can no longer distinguish whether the person in the photograph is lovely, or whether the old woman of the Yu family is truly detestable.

Advertisement: To Mr. Liang Boxin of Nanjing, Greetings. I am aware that you have developed hemoptysis due to excessive worry and have asked me to publish a notice seeking effective remedies. However, this matter is likely to lead to many abuses, and I dare not comply. Regarding your inquiry about the Yijin herb, I am not very clear. However, the wife of my colleague, Mr. Huang Jiping, suffered from hemoptysis last year and used this medicine, which she said was very effective. You might as well give it a try. Its distribution location is the Peisheng Pharmaceutical Company in Rendeli, Zhaozhou Road, outside the West Gate of Shanghai. This is specifically communicated to you, Yours sincerely, Ju Jingqi.

Local Customs Anecdotes

The Fierce Generals' Society of Dongshan 207

— Zhu Shaofei

In every village in Dongshan, one can see a Fierce Generals' Hall, with a plaque hanging high above the entrance, inscribed with the five golden characters "Upper Heaven King's Palace." If we were to tally all of Dongshan, there would be no more than twenty Fierce Generals Liu, but there are over sixty Fierce Generals' Halls. Because the villages are relatively large, one society would split into East Village and West Village, each building its own hall. When it is their turn to host the society, they carry Fierce General Liu to their own hall. That is why there are so many Fierce Generals' Halls.

The villagers' purpose in worshiping Fierce General Liu is generally to hope for a good silkworm harvest in their village, to pray for rain during droughts, and to carry Fierce General Liu out to drive away insects during insect plagues, which would immediately stop the infestation.

Every year during the old lunar New Year, the usually deserted Fierce Generals' Hall presents a lively scene, with lanterns and candles shining day and night, and incense burning vigorously. Even those who usually sit in small teahouses all day will squeeze into the Fierce Generals' Hall to join the excitement, only closing the doors again after thanking the general on the fifteenth day of the first month.

A full mountain circuit is a major event held by every society. Carrying the Fierce General Liu, who weighs several hundred pounds, they must pass through many high mountains and villages, with gongs beating in front and flags and umbrellas following. As they approach a village, the Fierce Generals' Hall in front of them sets up incense tables to welcome them, and they must spin around a few times on the threshing ground, signifying that they have paid their respects for the New Year. The members of the society can then rest and eat some soy beans boiled in soy sauce, pickles, tea, and so on.

On the ninth day of the first lunar month, there is a very dangerous competition to seize the society, which is a general gathering of the small Fierce Generals from various villages in the front mountains. Two tiger flags, marking the boundary line, are planted on the Tangzi Ridge in Chawan Village. The small Fierce Generals must line up according to their arrival time along the flag line. Around noon, the large yellow flag propped up against the big elm tree is shouldered by a strong man and run down the ridge as if flying, followed by each small sedan chair, twisting and turning down the ridge in a cloud of dust.

It is said that whichever village seizes the lead has a twelve-point certainty of a good silkworm harvest. But in their life-or-death struggle, some lose their shoes and socks, some fall and break their heads, and they often grab a handful of mud from the ground to apply to their wounds and continue the procession.

The customs of the Fierce Generals' Society in Dongshan are all, in a word, to pray that no famine will befall them. But in recent years, which village in Dongshan is not suffering from famine, and which villagers are not living in hunger? If Fierce General Liu could protect them, perhaps such a situation would not exist.

Shanghai Local Supplement of Shen Bao

Talking Points

Magic Glasses 208

— Jia

The Chinese are truly blessed. Foreign scientists, delving into their hearts and racking their brains, invent things one by one from scientific laboratories, such as electric lights, cars, airplanes, and movies, for our wealthy people to enjoy and utilize. It is unknown how many lifetimes of virtue the Chinese have cultivated to deserve such blessings.

When X-rays were first invented, I had an idea: if X-rays could be made into glasses and used for gambling, whether dice or mahjong tiles, everything could be seen through, giving one a monopoly on winning. Unfortunately, foreign scientists did not consider the needs of our Chinese people and did not invent such a thing. The Chinese, only knowing how to use but not invent, can only harbor such ideas, which is a great pity.

According to a Paris dispatch on the 24th, Auguste, a renowned physicist in his late seventies and one of the original inventors of film, has recently invented "magic glasses" that will greatly revolutionize movies. Auguste has found two colors from fifteen hundred colors, and used these to make glasses that allows the wearer to see real physical things when looking at a photograph, with the sensation of a subject matter. If you wear these two-color glasses to watch a movie, there is no difference from seeing real events. If there is a scene of a train speeding by in the movie, it will seem as if it is about to jump out of the screen and come straight at the viewer.

If these glasses arrive in Shanghai, business will surely flourish, and buyers will surely be enthusiastic. Because the Chinese are truly and deeply obsessed with movies. Even without these glasses, they watch until their eyes are blurred and their heads are dizzy, but they don't mind. If these glasses were available, no matter how expensive they were, even if it meant pawning their foot bindings, they would buy a pair of bifocals to wear. This is an inevitable trend.

I think these "magic glasses" still have some shortcomings. Their scope is too narrow, because these glasses only work when watching movies. If you use them to look at other things, they won't have any effect. I want to modify these glasses. If you could wear these glasses and see through the bizarre and erratic social conditions, the superficial and hypocritical psychology of the people, and the complex and ever-changing diplomatic policies of various countries, then these glasses would definitely be more valuable.

Or, even better, invent glasses that can transform anything. For example, if there is an ugly woman, she could wear the glasses and become a stunning beauty. If there is a heartbreaking event, wearing the glasses could turn it into a satisfying and gratifying one. Or, if there is an irreconcilable enemy, wearing the glasses could make them as close as brothers. I think if such glasses were invented, they would surely be even more profitable and widely welcomed.

Morning 209

— Hu Weixiong

Miscellaneous Notes from Rural Living (Part 2)

I slept soundly and woke up when the golden sunlight was peeking into the room. In the hall next door, the old lady was chanting Buddhist scriptures in a low voice. The murmuring sound seemed like rhythmic music. In the tranquil morning air, I understood and was reluctant to leave the warm bed, like a lover's whisper. My friend's study had four south-facing glass windows, and the sun gently crept to the center of the bed. I looked up to welcome this warmth, almost being lured back into a sweet slumber by the musical Buddhist chanting.

"Grandma, hasn't the Shanghai uncle gotten up yet?"

The seven-year-old child called out in the courtyard, so innocently. I wondered if he was surprised to see me get up late, or if he was not having enough fun playing alone and was thinking of me, his childlike uncle. His grandmother immediately stopped chanting and seemed to leave the sandalwood altar with burning candles to walk towards her grandson, forbidding him to speak in such a low voice. I jumped out of bed and they were peeking at me through the window.

The old lady first told her grandson to come in, and then said from outside the door, "You're disturbing your uncle's sleep. Children are so inconsiderate!"

"No, I woke up a while ago and was reading a few pages in bed." I lied, gently patting the child's head and asking, "Are you playing outside?"

"Really? Saying a child - I woke you up by chanting…"

"Not at all, not at all!" I said quickly and met her to go outside.

"Country people wake up early and have nothing to do, so they chant scriptures as a pastime, and now it's become a habit. Yunxun—my friend—always says I'm superstitious, but I just chant casually. How can the Bodhisattva care about such things?" she explained.

Huang Ma brought in a basin of water from the kitchen and interjected, "Madam even wants to cultivate a granddaughter!"

The madam did not object, a satisfied smile revealing her kind corner of her mouth. As if something had been said that she felt right in her heart, she went along with it and said, "The young master's breakfast is all prepared, and it will be moved to the study in a while."

A mother's love stirred in my memory. When I was a child, I lost my biological parents and grew up at my sister and her husband's house, and did not have a brilliant childhood and did not know of the greatness of a mother's love. I used my own physical strength to support myself, and my life was simply fish on the chopping block. How could I ask for some warm, maternal love?

Breakfast was rich, all country dishes that could be stored for a long time. It was probably specially prepared for a respected guest, right? It was still early, and I wanted to take a walk nearby, but the child came to pull me to the orchard behind the house.

Behind Jishantang, after passing through a side alley, there was his family's kitchen, which was also a row of three rooms. Going out through the small door on the left, was a large orchard that combined a vegetable garden and a flower garden. Vegetables were planted nearby. Huang Ma told me that they could not finish eating these few vegetable beds even in the winter.

Stepping on the moist clay, we stood under a plum tree. The tree was in full bloom with dignified pale white flowers. The aroma of these flowerballs wafted to my nose and involuntarily opened up both hands and took a deep breath. The doctor had advised me to have such an open space for my recuperation. Thank God for giving me this beautiful place.

The garden was surrounded by a row of low walls, as if touring famous scenic spots. At the corner of the wall were a dozen peach trees, not yet in bloom, already coquettishly shaking their waists. Allow me to live through this spring, I pray to Heaven.

The child was much happier with a companion and jumped around happily, telling many innocent stories, until his grandmother called him to study.

Quarrying 210

— Wu Fei

The sky had barely brightened when wisps of smoke were already rising from the rooftops of houses in the vicinity of Gushan and Guishan.

Jinlin's wife at Xiaoyao Palace got up earlier than anyone else today. When she got out of bed, it was still dark outside, and she had to light the kerosene lamp to do things.

"Debao's father! Get up! The rice is cooked." She called to Jinlin, who was sleeping like a dead pig in bed, but was afraid of waking the child who was only one year old in the corner of the bed! Debao! So she called out in a very low voice. However, Jinlin carried a heavy iron hammer all day long, desperately working in the stone shoal, and his body was indeed somewhat unsustainable. Especially at night, he just wanted to use this sleep to make up for the energy he lost; therefore, his wife pushed and called him several times, but he still did not move at all, and still slept soundly.

"It's dawn! Everyone has eaten their mountain-going meal and gone to the mine; if you don't get up, the first turn in your own mine has to be opened early, loaded up and sold..." She was impatient with shouting and mumbled, importantly pinching his nose, "Get up!"

"Ugh! Is it dawn? I'm so tired! My bones feel like they're split apart!" He turned over when his wife pinched his nose, felt the aching bones, but finally struggled to get up.

"The sun is three feet high! Uncle Agou, Grandpa Huangmao, they have all gone up the mountain; tired, who doesn't know what tired is! It's all for the three meals and a bowl of rice!"

"Oh! They've already gone!" He quickly washed his face, sat down at the broken plank table, and gulped down two large bowls of rice in a few bites, and rushed to the mountain with his iron hammer and iron rod. When he arrived at the mine, he saw that Changsheng, Jinhua, Aquan, Maogou, Fulin, and others who worked in rotation with him had arrived before him, and they were sitting on the rocks puffing on their pipes.

"You guys have already come!" Jinlin stepped forward, put the iron hammer and iron rod on his shoulder on the ground, took a breath and said.

"We're here! Are we going to start by working on the surface today, or are we going to mine the turn first?" Everyone asked him as usual.

"I think we should mine the turn first! Anyway, there's no way out on the surface." Jinlin put one foot on a stone, pondered for a while, and pointed to a stone peak of four or five thousand tons and said to them.

"Alas! If this turn of white stone were ten years ago, I'm afraid it would be worth no less than two hundred dollars. I remember that at that time, several women on the surface even wore gold rings so that they couldn't even bend their fingers. Those who owned mines, supported stone boats, and mined mountains, which one didn't eat big fish and meat every day, wearing fur and silk? When gambling started during the New Year, the stakes were easily talked about in thousands or hundreds. Alas! Now, it’s almost impossible to fill our stomachs. It’s hard to believe!" A-Da indeed felt a lot of emotion about the differences between the past and now, so he complained about the turn.

"Hey! Now this job is too crowded, how can it be compared with the past? Now even with the goods, we are still worried that we can't sell them! Sometimes we can't even make enough for our labor costs!" Jinlin couldn't help but feel a little sad!

They smoked for a while, as if gathering all the energy in their bodies by the power of the smoke, everyone shook off their spirits, took the tools they should use, and walked up the rock.

"Umph! Ah ha! Oh yo!" Everyone's strength was concentrated on the iron hammer and iron rod, and everyone's spirit was used on this majestic and great call.

Bang - bang - bang - stone chips flew into the sky, and stone fragments jumped to the distance. Muscles swelled inside their bodies, and sweat dripped on their bodies!

"Umph! Ah ha! Oh yo!" Everyone was screaming! Screaming…

The entire valley was shaken!

Note - A "turn" is a stone mountain. After it is mined, it must be tied with rotating wood to drag it down the mountain. A "surface" is a rock on a hill or ground surface. The people moving it can be 2, 4, or even over 10 people, meaning that it can be carried. A "shasha pian" (煞片) is a stone fragment weighing fifty or sixty catties.

Mom! Isn't there food to eat here?

— Yu Yan

Child Bride 211

— Yonghui

"Mom, I'm not going! I'm definitely not going!" the girl said, agitated, the muscles on her face etched into wrinkles by extreme discomfort, her body falling into her mother's arms. "I can't stand my mother-in-law's (note: the husband's mother) beatings. When my mother-in-law beats people, she has no sense of proportion, and it's always a beating with a wooden stick! Mom, look at me... this whole body..." The girl took off her top, revealing stripes of red and purple crisscrossing her back. The extreme wounds, seen in the eyes of onlookers, would move anyone to tears.

"Good child, listen to your mother and go! Your mother has no choice, and cannot bear to leave you! If not for being unable to feed... you..." the mother said, becoming more and more anxious and uncomfortable. She felt very guilty, clearly seeing the welts on her daughter's body, clearly knowing that the girl could not bear it, but she herself was telling her daughter to go back obediently. Wasn't she herself announcing her daughter's death sentence? "Good child, I will definitely try to bring you back next year, as long as the fields aren't as bad as they are this year, if there's any way at all," the mother comforted.

"No, I won't! I definitely won't go back! You said last year that you would bring me back when there was a harvest, but it's still not happened..."

"Good child, don't blame your mother. Your mother only gave you to others to be a young bride because there was no food at home!"

"No food to eat? But my younger brother has food to eat!" The girl said somewhat angrily.

"Good child, how can you say such a thing? Saying it this way, it seems like your mother is biased!" the mother explained gently, "You girls can't compare to boys! Boys are for carrying on the family line! How did your father tell me when he passed away? He wanted me to teach and raise your brother well, and to keep your brother with me even if I had to eat grass roots and tree bark. The Wang family's incense depends entirely on your brother alone!"

"..." The girl had no words to say, perhaps tacitly acknowledging that her mother's words were correct?

A twelve-year-old girl should be innocent and lively as a matter of course; but for some reason, she has a very old heart! Perhaps it was the extreme suffering and inhuman life that has aged her like this!

At night, the moonlight was like water, and all sounds were silent. This should be good poetic material for poets, but our girl was bound by terrifying memories.

It was a misty autumn morning, the fog so thick that you could barely see your fingers in front of you, but the twelve-year-old child bride groped her way to the edges of her own fields to pull weeds from the soybean seedlings.

The fog did not dissipate until two hours after breakfast. She was about to rest after a morning of hard work.

Perhaps she had been squatting on the ground for too long. She suddenly stood up, and her foot twisted, crushing a soybean seedling, though she herself did not realize it.

"You low-life bitch, a belly full of bad ideas! When you saw that I told you to pull weeds, you deliberately crushed the soybean seedlings! See if I don't beat you to death!" This sudden sound really startled her too much! She was as afraid as a mouse hearing a cat meow, her whole body trembling. Then, a wooden stick fell on her head, back, and feet...

It is unknown when that fierce beating stopped, because she fainted before twenty blows.

It was already two o'clock after midnight! Less than a few hours before dawn; after dawn, she would have to go to her mother-in-law's house. The old wounds from the past two days still hurt on her body, and perhaps in a few days, new pains would come to replace the slightly faded old pains! She dared not think, but had to think.

The face of her mother-in-law seemed to float in the darkness: those thick eyebrows, the wide mouth with hideous yellow teeth, the fleshy face, that ghost-like shriek...

"Dead ghost, you're only back today! Why didn't you die

Page 21

at your mother's house!" She guessed that her mother-in-law's opening words upon seeing her would be like this.

Scenery of the South 212

— Jiang Yuanding

Water is a Genius

In geography books, the so-called "floating market streets" of Wuzhou in the South are highlighted as a characteristic. In fact, these things do not hold special meaning to people from Wuzhou, perhaps because of "familiarity." However, there is another kind of miracle that people from Wuzhou may not be aware of. However, I think this should be the best scenery in the South.

On the right bank of the Tan River, stands White Crane Mountain. The hilltop is Hebin Park, with pine forests, palm trees, and sun-shading banyan trees. No matter how hot and humid the summer is, it is always a cool world there.

When we stand in the shade of the trees and gaze, we can see that Wuzhou is surrounded on three sides by the Li River and the West River. The two rivers converge in front of us, and the people of Wuzhou have given it a special name, called the "Mandarin Duck River."

Because the Li River is emerald green and the West River is yellow and turbid, after the two bodies of water converge, they exchange and become a beautiful picture. Because of the distance, one cannot see the flow of water, and the river surface becomes a still eddy. If you appreciate it carefully, you will recognize many cartoons. In the yellow and turbid water, a touch of green is mixed in, or green surrounds a band of yellow, often forming dissolving, elongated women's hair, or a range of distant mountains, and other various images, which are very rich in symbolic poetry. Compared with the fleeting, stagnant cloud shadows in the sky, it is even more lively.

If you admit that clouds are geniuses, then you should also admit that water is a genius.

News: The Bubble Society is an organization formed by young people who love literature and art. Its purpose is to connect feelings, exchange knowledge, study literature and art, and increase public interest in literature and art. Members are divided into basic and ordinary types. Copies of the articles of association are available upon request. Regardless of gender, anyone who is interested in literature and art is welcome to join.

Ballad Singing 214

Jiang Ruting Zhu Jiesheng Falling Golden Fan

Zhonghua (1140) 9:00 PM to 9:45 PM

Opening Chapter "Lament of a Courtesan"

In the gentle and clear fourth month, the rain has just cleared, the courtyard is desolate and I am heartbroken. From ancient times, people's feelings have been cold and warm, and the glamour of courtesans is only temporary. Before I was a woman, I moved people's hearts, holding hands and touching feet, and words of affection came from the mouth. At fifteen or sixteen, the flower is just blooming, like the moon at Mid-Autumn Festival, exceptionally bright. At seventeen or eighteen, everyone loves me, like a lotus emerging from the water, fragrant and fresh. At twenty, it is the height of spring, and the oriole shuttles and the sparrow is trained. There are many carriages and horses in front of the door, and the old madam is like a pearl in the palm. Morning is cold and night is clear, and romantic young men come like clouds. Outside the door, a prince is about to mount his horse, and it is reported that a young master is coming soon. We are close and happy with each other, and there is no end to the false warmth. But now the flower is withered and the moon has set, and I am no longer as moving as I was in the past. There are only a few lonely carriages and horses in front of the door, and the pearl in the palm has turned to dust. There is no shadow of anyone on the Cold Food Festival and Qingming Festival, and the romantic young men are nowhere to be seen. Where have the dissolute young men gone? The elegant young masters do not come to the door. Who will love her, and what false warmth is left? Thinking about it makes me very sad.

Yao Xiao'an Wang Pingqiu Qilin Leopard

Zhongxi (1040) 11:00 PM to 12:00 AM

Opening Chapter "By the West Lake"

Hangzhou is known for its tranquility and elegance. The setting sun shines on the West Lake. Emperor Gaozong of the Southern Song Dynasty once camped here, and nine emperors made it their capital, known as the king. The scenery is indeed secluded and beautiful, and the scenery is pleasant everywhere. Don't you see the clear mountains and rivers where crows and magpies are chattering? Feilai Peak faces Taoguang. Admire the three peaks of Tianzhu. The majestic and majestic Ten Thousand Buddhas are hidden. The Three Pools Mirroring the Moon have become classics. Willow catkins fly on the Bai Su Causeway. Everyone stops here when they see the whip, in order to see the scenery of the lakes and mountains. It is true that Xizi did not live in vain in this life, and because of the name of the sparrow, it will be famous forever. He should laugh happily in the Nine Springs, and the eternal regrets will be relieved. It's a pity that the beggar Zixu became a dream, and the King of Wu cried for him at the platform. It's a pity that he cut off his head with his white hair, leaving behind a hatred that hurts his teeth for thousands of years. Therefore, every time autumn comes, he takes revenge, and the tide surges towards Qiantang. His heart is angry because of Xishi's plan, and he died innocently, losing his life. This led to the loss of Jiangshan Wu Yue, and the regret of thousands of years is long. Although Xizi sailed away in a boat, he returned to the mountains and hid his shadow. Doctor Wu was so angry that his hair stood on end, so he surged and showed his madness. It has been passed down to this day for thousands of years, and it is regarded as a strange and beautiful sight. Who knows the loyal guests of the past? Dan Chen's great spirit reported to the King of Wu. A burst of anger is Shiqiantang.

Shanghai Shenbao Supplement Movie Special Issue

Tarzan is Coming Again! Original Work Makes a Fortune 218

— Chen Xiong

Last year (1934) in September, when "Tarzan and His Mate" premiered in this city and broke the premiere record for Western films, Tarzan's name had already been deeply imprinted in the minds of ordinary movie fans.

The production of Tarzan films began nineteen years ago—in 1916, the first Tarzan film was released to the world—and up to the recent "Tarzan and His Mate," it has been brought to the screen twelve times. Because each Tarzan film can make a profit, especially "Tarzan the Ape Man" and "Tarzan and His Mate," and the latter was selected as one of the top ten films of last year, MGM recently bought the thirteenth Tarzan script from the original author, preparing to make another Tarzan beast film this year. Of course, the male and female leads will be Weissmuller and Maureen O'Sullivan, whom movie fans are eager to see.

Tarzan is not only famous in the film industry, but in the American wireless broadcasting industry, Tarzan has become a drama adopted by various broadcasting stations; he is also a common pen comic seen by countless newspaper readers, as well as a trademark for dozens of daily necessities such as chewing gum, garters, and plastic toys. Whatever author, they would all be willing to be the owner of Tarzan. Tarzan will certainly bring fame and fortune to his owner, but who else can enjoy these rights besides the original author, Edgar Rice Burroughs?

Burroughs was not originally an author. Before 1912, he was a cavalryman, a railway inspector, a gold digger, a salesman of proprietary medicines, and a consultant for store services. In 1910, Burroughs heard from a friend that the rewards for writers were very generous. So he began his writing career, selling articles to various magazines and newspapers for manuscript fees. In 1912, he first published his first Tarzan novel called "Tarzan of the Apes." In the silent film era, a film company adapted it into a film and renamed it "Tarzan the Mighty," starring the strongman Elmo Lincoln. This "Tarzan the Mighty" was one of the silent films that grossed over a million dollars. So Burroughs saw that his Tarzan novel was indeed popular, so he abandoned everything and decided to devote all his efforts to writing novels.

Ten years later, in 1922, Burroughs felt that his novel publishers were exploiting too much commission, so he organized the Burroughs Company to print and sell his own products himself. After Burroughs first succeeded in writing the Tarzan novel in 1913, fortunately he had some foresight and registered the name Tarzan with the Patent Office early on, and has since enjoyed the benefits of the patent steadily.

Burroughs is now almost sixty years old, but he looks like a strong man in his forties or fifties. He goes horseback riding and plays tennis in the suburbs every day. He learned to fly a plane a few months ago and now has his own private plane. He has a son who has inherited his father's business and manages all the administrative affairs of the Burroughs Company.

Although Burroughs' Tarzan is set in Africa, people who have read his novels all think that Burroughs must be very familiar with the customs and conditions of Africa. In fact, this writer who is famous for writing African novels has never been to Africa.

Film Review

Review of "The Band Plays On" 219

— Ling He

The Band Plays On

—Nanjing—

In the past, we have come into contact with many American sports films. At the same time, we have pointed out that those films, like the works with airplanes and rowing as themes, use ball games as the main theme. It is nothing more than making the film proceed in a tense atmosphere, so that the audience can obtain a stimulating effect, and there is no other significance. However, now the same type of work, "The Band Plays On," is a better one. This is not to say that its content is so substantial, but rather that it is quite successful in terms of production techniques.

Like every ordinary film, the story here is entrusted to fantasy, making four wandering children become four football stars. However, what is more characteristic is that the playwright writes the four of them very affectionately, and then constructs a love entanglement in the middle. Therefore, this film has a very good achievement in terms of emotional grasp.

The usual American films often have a kind of lively and enterprising youthful spirit, and what cannot be missing is also humor and comedy, which are naturally not missing here. These are organized with the tense atmosphere of the football field, which has already made us feel that the director can indeed do the job happily. However, these are not the characteristics of the film. What we have to point out is the tragedy of Katie's love between Tony and Stephen. When Tony accidentally sees Katie kissing Stephen, his pain, from the declaration of concession in the ward to taking the wrong road after leaving the ward, we have connected this scene with the scene where Stephen sends the leather suitcase to Katie and Katie scolds Tony after Stephen is injured. We are moved by it. In addition, the five of them are in the countryside, some playing chess, some playing leaf games, and lightly depicting Stephen and Katie's love and play, Tony's sentimental solitary walk, Katie chasing after him, those two scenes, whether it is the atmosphere or emotion, have very good achievements.

From these places, we can certainly see the success of the director. At the same time, the main actors, such as Stuart Erwin, who plays Stephen, and the reporter in "Viva Liberty" have the same personality. His excellent acting skills can be appreciated by anyone. Also, the heroine Betty Furness, who met for the first time, also performed very well. She is so full of emotion that she naturally and deeply depicts the personality of the characters in the play.

Others, such as Tony, did not have any achievements in previous films, but he also performed well here, which shows that the director Russell Mack has a very good grasp of the actors.

"Forsaking All Others" Co-Starring Three Big Stars 220

— Dai

This is indeed a rare opportunity. "Forsaking All Others" co-starring Joan Crawford, Clark Gable, and Robert Montgomery, three big stars, will meet us at the Nanjing Grand Theater. This film has been recognized as one of MGM's best.

Joan Crawford plays the female lead. What a beloved star she is! Clark Gable and Robert Montgomery are also two very popular male stars. You can imagine how well "Forsaking All Others" will do with three people working together.

The magnificence of the scenery and the outstanding performance are all above the standard. In addition to the three big stars, the remaining supporting roles are also famous figures in the film industry. Director W. S. Van Dyke is one of the most famous directors in Hollywood today. Under his handling, this film will certainly be even more perfect.

The story is taken from a comedy depicting a scene of a love triangle. Gable and Joan have been lovers since childhood. On the eve of her return to New York from Spain, when they parted sadly on the park road, she also expressed her willingness to marry him, but he knew that Montgomery was his rival in love.

The next day, he received a telegram from Montgomery saying that he had married a girl. A year later, Joan, who was in love with Gable, suddenly fell in love with Montgomery. After a few weeks of Gable's pursuit, she finally agreed to drive with him to the countryside. Many interesting details are inserted into the scene where the car breaks down. All three protagonists perform to the best of their ability.

Jinda Drama Society's "Wet Paint" Public Performance 221

The long-awaited public performance of the Jinda Drama Society has been scheduled for 7:00 pm on March 1st at the Zhenhe Jinda University Auditorium. The script is the famous comedy "Wet Paint" by French playwright Rene Fauchois. This performance has been rehearsed for nearly two months. In order to be as perfect and excellent as possible, it was once extended. The results should be amazing and worthy of being called a unique performance in China's theater world. Those who hold positions are mostly famous figures in the domestic drama world at the time, such as the director Mr. Ouyang Yuqian, the stage supervisor Mr. Ying Yunwei, and the actors Wang Ying, Zuo Ming, Li Lilian, Shu Xiuwen, Shu, Lulu, etc. It is said that it will be officially performed in this city in mid-March (the date and location will be announced after confirmation). After the performance, it will go to Nanjing to perform at the invitation of a theater.

Movie Novel

Schoolboy's Loving Mother (Grand Old Girl) (4) 224

— Shu Min

Lulan Bels laughed; "That's not it. I came specifically to see you again." Ded asked strangely: "Have you seen me for thirty years, isn't that enough?" Lulan said: "I thought so... but... maybe I'm wrong... I often think to myself that a gambler must also be a bold and just person, willing to sacrifice everything in order to win a greater victory..." Ded interrupted: "Gambling is originally a profession, the same as other professions." Lulan Bels seemed to be touched and said: "But my uncle—Saradu Gabels—is different." Ded asked in surprise: "Your uncle!" Lulan Bels ignored him and continued to talk to himself; "I often saw him throwing six naturals in a row, but he always bet all of them, until he won completely, and I lost all my money."

Ded was surprised and opened his eyes wide when he heard this and said: "Hey, you talk like an expert." Lulan said sadly: "After suffering all the hardships, one can become a superior person. These things are experiences gained from being fooled. It is good to throw a natural, but it is icy cold to throw a pair of snake eyes." Ded exclaimed in surprise: "Holy Markrull!" Lulan continued to say endlessly: "So I want to see you again. I have always admired your gambling integrity, but I am very disappointed. You are just an iron horn, specializing in throwing copper coins."

Ded jumped up and said: "Listen up! I dare to gamble with you anytime, anywhere, no matter how big or small!" Lulan deliberately teased him and said: "Two hundred and fifty, all at once, okay?" Ded listened and froze for a moment and said: "That's too much." Lulan put on a disdainful look and said: "I thought you were a real gambler." Ded straightened his back and said: "Of course. How much money do you have, I will play with you." Lulan said: "Just two hundred and fifty yuan." Ded looked at her. She knew that her dice were reliable, so she agreed decisively. He stood up and laughed and said: "Miss Bels, this is what you wanted. Okay, let's go to the chance hall."

As he said that, he took the lead and walked towards the famous "back room." But when he reached the door, he stopped again and said: "No, I won't fall for your trick again. Your hands are too fast, and you want to grab things." Lulan said: "Clarence, I'm afraid that's not possible anymore. I conceded last time, what else is there to say? I just want some cash now so that I can go out. Like my uncle, I would rather bet the whole amount and win or lose all at once." Ded listened and seemed to feel that it was unbearable to win the old woman's money. However, this was a business that she had brought to his door, so how could he send the God of Wealth back? Besides, two hundred and fifty yuan is not a small amount. So he shrugged his shoulders.

Ded entered the "back room" and went to open the drawer to take the dice. Lulan quickly opened her bag, took out a check, threw it on the table, and took out her two dice and asked politely: "Shall I be the dealer?" Ded was still searching for his special dice, but Lulan asked again: "Let me use my own dice... I'm used to it, and my luck is better...:" As she said that, her voice trembled. She then smiled, seeming rather pitiful. Ded thought that she might not win with one throw, so he agreed readily, and immediately took out a roll of banknotes and asked: "How much are you betting?"

Lulan said: "I'm betting the whole amount." She held the dice in her hand, shaking them near her ear like an expert, blowing a breath, and shouting: "Dice, be good... baby is going to buy a pair of shoes..." She moved her hand forward, and the two dice rolled out. She immediately shouted: "Holy Dijerti! A natural! Ride a good horse!" Ded had no choice, and a large part of the roll of banknotes had already been lost. He threw the rest on the table, and Lulan picked up the dice as before, shaking them near her ear, blowing a breath, and then shouting: "Dice! Get hot!" (To be continued)
